Yaŋsop aŋyomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨŋ dekgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen yaŋ mandabi: ‘Nak dakon yut uŋun amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun da abɨŋ bɨsit aŋnamni do tosak.’ Mani ji da kulabɨk aba ‘kabo noknok dakon pasɨlɨ tamo asak.’ ”
Pɨdaŋba kɨno! Kabɨt, uwal da kɨsiron nepjak amɨn kɨlɨ abɨk.”
Buŋon Erodias da Jon aŋakba kɨmotjak uŋun dakon kosit kagɨt. Altok altok bɨsapnikon Erot da jap noknok ak do amɨn madep paŋmuwukgɨt. Gapman dakon pi amɨn madep ae emat amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨni ae Galili mɨktɨm dakon kɨla amɨn kɨsi paŋmuwukgɨt.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak gen kobogɨ tagɨsi yosol, do koŋ gwago kɨlɨ yɨpmaŋ dek, do tobɨlek yutgokon kɨŋek koki.”
Aŋakwa amɨn morapmɨ da Yesu do top sɨtnok genyo yaŋba geni dakon kosirɨ dɨma pɨsagɨt.
Koŋ uŋun Yesu da nandaŋ yoban bɨt da butgwan pɨgɨni do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit.
Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdet, gak gen bamɨ yogok amɨn yaŋ nandamaŋ. Gak amɨn do dɨma pasoldol. Amɨn mani toŋ ae amɨn mani mɨni uŋun kɨsi Piŋkop dakon aŋpak yoyɨŋ dek mudosol. Gak niaŋ nandɨsal? Sisa do moneŋ ɨmno tagɨ asak bo dɨma? Ɨmneŋ bo dɨma?”
Yoyɨŋban paŋdetni da gen uŋun iyɨ gɨn yaŋ nandaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Kɨmoron da pɨdot pɨdot uŋun yo kɨnda nido nandaŋek yosok.”
Mani amɨn kɨnda da Telagɨ Wup abɨŋ yɨp do manji gen kɨnda yosak kaŋ, Piŋkop da dɨwarɨni dɨma wɨrɨrɨtjak. Uŋun dɨmasisi, uŋun dɨwarɨni mudok mudogɨ mɨni taŋ wɨgɨkdɨsak.”
“Yesu, Nasaret amɨn, gak nibaŋ aŋnim do nandɨsal? Nin paŋupbal ak do abɨl? Nak nandaŋ gamɨsat, gak Piŋkop Dakon Telagɨ Amɨni.”
Ae dabɨlgo da yokwi aki do gayɨŋban kaŋ, dabɨlgo pɨlɨkgi. Gwɨnɨmbɨl egek Tɨpdomon kɨndap tebanon pɨgɨki yaŋ do dabɨlgo kɨnda pɨlɨgek tagapmɨ Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asagon tagɨ wɨgɨki.
Yaŋban koŋ da madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek monjɨ uŋun maban bumjot yombem pagakwan koŋ yɨpmaŋek wɨŋ kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da monjɨ kaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Kuŋwakni.”
Iyɨŋban Pailat da emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn yaŋ ɨban opban iyɨgɨt, “Asi Yesu kuŋwak, bo dɨma?”
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da gen tebaisi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak gen dɨma yaŋek amɨn on yɨpmaŋ det!”
Aŋek kokup pap bo kokup monɨŋ ae dukwan dukwan kɨgɨt amɨn da sot amɨn muwut muwut tamokon uŋudon paŋabɨŋ yopgwit. Aŋek paba pɨgɨk dɨwatnikon ɨgayɨni do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit. Yaŋ ɨgayɨwit amɨn uŋun kɨlek taŋ mudawit.
Aŋek kokup amɨn kɨsi morap yut uŋun da yomakon muwukgwit.
Ji Piŋkop da papiakon gen tosok uŋun dɨma manjɨŋ nandawit? Gen uŋun yaŋ: ‘Yut agak amɨn da gwak yokwi yaŋ yaŋek maba kɨgɨt, uŋun gwak amɨn da yut kodɨgɨkon tɨp kɨnda naŋ tɨdawit da akdak.
Uŋun amɨn bamot pɨndagek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Abɨŋ nak nolgɨl, aŋakwal amɨn tɨmɨt tɨmɨt dakon kosit dolɨko.”
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yagɨt, “Moses uŋun but tebanji do aŋek gen teban uŋun mandagɨt.
Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Dɨwarɨ da gak do Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn yaŋ yoŋ, ae dɨ da Elaija yaŋ yoŋ, ae dɨ da kombɨ amɨn kɨnda kalɨp egɨpgut uŋun da pɨdak da egɨsak yaŋ yoŋ.”
Gen yaŋ yaŋban Erot burɨ wagɨl yokwi tagɨt. Mani amɨn jap nawit uŋun da ɨŋamon yaŋ teban tok gen yagɨt uŋun kɨrɨŋɨt do mayak taŋek gen yagɨt uŋun dɨma kɨrɨŋɨkgɨt.
Yaŋ aŋek Kwen Kokup sɨŋtaŋek yaŋba kɨk aŋek iyɨgɨt, “Epata!” (Uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ “Pɨsoki!”)
Yaŋban iyɨwit, “Moses da yaŋ mandagɨt: Amɨn kɨnda mɨŋatni kwɨnɨt do kaŋ, mɨŋat paŋkwɨnɨt papia kɨnda mandaŋ ɨmɨŋek kwɨnɨtjak.”
Ae uŋun amɨn da tuŋon amɨn emarɨ toŋ abɨdokdaŋ, ae pakbi emarɨ toŋ naŋba uŋun da dɨma paŋupbal akdaŋ. Uŋun amɨn da sot amɨn kɨsirɨ kwenikon wɨtjɨŋba sotni mudokdaŋ.”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, nak wain ae dɨma naŋek egɨ wɨgɨ Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Agak kokupmon don wain kalugɨ nokeŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek tɨlak gen kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda kokup kɨndakon kɨk do aŋek oman amɨni do pi kokwinɨk yomɨŋek yut dakon kɨla ani do yoyɨsak. Aŋek yoma sopsop dakon kɨla amɨn yoma kɨlani tebai asak do iyɨsak.
Jon telagɨ pakbi sogɨt bɨsapmon, Piŋkop da yabekban pi agɨt, bo amɨn da yabekba agɨt? Uŋun do nayɨni.”
“Ae amɨn kɨnda pigaga egɨpjak kaŋ, yutnon ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkni kɨŋ abɨdok do dɨmasi kɨsak.
Yesu dubagɨkon akban kaŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek Yesu da buron kɨŋ gawak ɨmgut.
Aŋakwa Parisi amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Pɨndat, amɨn Sabat bɨsapmon nido gen teban yapmaŋek pi aŋ?”
Amɨn kɨnda nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨŋek telagɨ pakbi sosak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn Kwen Kokup do amɨn asak. Ae amɨn kɨnda nak dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ namjak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn Tɨpdom do amɨn asak.
Kombɨ amɨn Aisaia da gen yaŋ mandagɨt: “Nandani, geno yaŋ teŋteŋosak do amɨn kɨnda yabekgo uŋun da mibɨltaŋ gamjak. Aŋek kositgo aŋnoman asak.
IIyɨŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda da mɨŋatni yɨpmaŋek kɨŋ mɨŋat kalugɨ pasak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn yumabi asak.
Kosirɨ kɨnda 50 ae kosirɨ kɨnda 100 yaŋ yɨk aŋaŋ kɨwit.
Aŋakwa gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn Jerusalem kokup papmon da apgwit uŋun da Yesu do yaŋ yawit, “Koŋ dakon amɨn tagɨni Belsebul uŋun da burɨgwan egakwan uŋun dakon tapmɨmon da koŋ yoldak.”
“Wain sop pakpak bɨsap kwaŋ taŋakwan oman monjɨ kɨnda yabekban wain bamɨ tɨmɨk paŋopjak do kɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban amɨn dɨwarɨ kapmatjok akgwit uŋun nandaŋek yawit, “Nandaŋ, uŋun Elaija do yaŋ ɨmɨsak.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon yo jɨgɨsi altokdaŋ. Piŋkop da yo morap wasagɨron da egɨ abɨsok ekwamaŋon yo jɨgɨsi uŋuden kɨnda dɨma altagɨt. Ae buŋon yo jɨgɨ uŋuden aeni dɨma altokdaŋ.
Aŋakwan oman mɨŋatjok uŋun da Pita aeni kaŋek amɨn uŋudon akgwit yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On amɨn uŋun Yesu da kabɨkon nani kɨnda.”
Gen uŋun yaŋba nandaŋek ɨmalni kukwaŋ yɨpmaŋek Yesukon opgut.
Gen uŋun da tɨlagon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn Jon da mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon kɨŋ altagɨt. Altaŋek but tobɨl aŋek telagɨ pakbi soŋakwa Piŋkop da dɨwarɨni yopmaŋ yomjak do yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Sisa dakon yo uŋun Sisa iyɨ do ɨmni, ae Piŋkop dakon yo uŋun Piŋkop iyɨ do ɨmni.” Gen uŋun yaŋban nandaŋek Yesu do nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Yaŋban koŋ da amɨn uŋun ukwayɨgek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yɨpmaŋ degek wɨŋ kɨgɨt.
Aŋakwa mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep Yesu kaŋek but galak nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn Yesukon kɨŋek “Gɨldat tagɨ!” yaŋ iyɨwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji pik kɨndap kaŋek butji pɨsosak. Kɨlɨŋɨ pakbini toŋ ae tamɨ kaluk yopmaŋdak, uŋun bɨsapmon gɨldat bɨsap kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandaŋ.
Yaŋban iyɨ gɨn notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Kobogɨ ni gen kɨnda naŋ iyɨneŋ? ‘Piŋkop da yabekgɨt’ yaŋ iyɨneŋ kaŋ, gen tebai yaŋ niyɨsak, ‘Ji nido dɨma nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmgwit?’
Yaŋ aŋakwa Yesu da nandaŋ gadatni kaŋek amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Monjɨ, dɨwarɨgo yopmaŋ gamɨsat.”
Aŋek nandaŋ gadatni mɨni do, uŋun do nandaban ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt. Yaŋ nandaŋek kokup taŋ aŋaŋ kɨwit uŋudon kɨŋ Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋ dekgɨt.
Mɨktɨm da mudosak bɨsap madep tepmɨ dɨma apdɨsak. Mibɨltok amɨn mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun da Gen Bin Tagɨsi nandani.
Yaŋ kaŋek tɨp kɨnamgwan pɨgɨ wɨli gɨmoŋɨ kɨnda kawit. Uŋun ɨlɨkba pɨgɨk kwakwagɨ dubagɨ kɨnda pabi da amɨnsi tet do yɨkban kawit. Kaŋek wurɨpdagek pasalgwit.
Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ gat ae Erot da kabɨkon amɨn dɨwarɨ gat da Yesu dakon gen nandaŋek suŋ kɨnda yaŋban abɨdoni do kɨla amɨn da yabekgwit.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ amɨn da Gen Bin Tagɨsi yoyɨŋek mɨŋat on da yo ak uŋun dakon gen bin kɨsi yoyɨŋakwa nandakdaŋ. Aŋek uŋun mɨŋat dakon man bini dɨma pasɨldɨsak.”
Yaŋ yaŋek tobɨl paŋdetni kapbɨ egɨpgwiron kɨŋ pɨndakban dɨpmɨn pakgwit. Pɨndagek Pita yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Saimon, gak dɨpmɨn pokdol, ma? Bɨsap awa kaloŋɨ da arɨpmon gɨn nak gat Piŋkop do nandaŋek dɨma egɨpneŋ?
Amɨn kɨnda jikon da mibɨltok amɨn egɨp do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn mɨŋat amɨn morap dakon oman amɨni egek mibɨltok amɨn tagɨ egɨpjak.
Aŋek Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da gen kɨnda yaŋ yoŋ ‘Elaija mibɨltok abɨŋakwan Kristo buŋon apjak.’ Gen uŋun nido yoŋ?”
Tepmɨ abɨŋ dandaban dɨpmɨn potni kaŋ, uŋun tagɨ dɨma.
Iyɨŋba nandaŋek Yesu uŋun boron wɨgakwan amɨn koŋ gat egɨpgut uŋun da Yesu yol do bɨsit tebai iyɨgɨt.
Ji teban taŋek bɨsit aŋek egɨpni. Yaŋ aŋek egɨpni kaŋ, paŋkewalon arɨpmɨ dɨma moni. But da nak nol do galak tosok mani gɨp dakon teban tokni mɨni.”
Wɨŋ kɨŋakwan amɨn da uŋun kaŋek wurɨpdagek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Mao, uŋun ni yo kɨnda da altosok? On amɨn gen ŋwakŋwarɨsi yosok. Amɨn mani toŋ da tɨlagon yosok. Koŋ gen yoyɨŋban geni guramɨkgaŋ.”
Yo amɨn but nandak nandagon da wɨsak uŋun yaŋ: nandak nandak yokwi, yumabi aŋpak mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ, yo kabo, amɨn dapdap,
Kɨŋ 3 kilok aŋakwan Yesu da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Eloi, eloi lama sabaktani?” Gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ yaŋ: “Piŋkopno, Piŋkopno, nido nepmaŋ dekdal?”
nido Erot da Jon do pasalek yaŋ nandagɨt, “Jon uŋun amɨn kɨlegɨ ae telagɨsi.” Yaŋ nandaŋek si aŋkutnagɨt. Erot da Jon dakon gen nandaŋek but morap agɨt, mani geni nandak do galak tagɨt.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Meŋno padɨk padɨkno uŋun namɨn?”
Yaŋ aban Yesu da datni iyɨgɨt, “Bɨsap niaŋ da yaŋ agɨt?” Yaŋban datni da yagɨt, “Ŋakŋagɨkon da altaŋ ɨmgut da tosok.
Yaŋban paŋdetni si pasalek iyɨ gɨn yawit, “On niaŋen amɨn kɨnda da mɨrɨm ae pakbiyo yoyɨŋban geni guramɨkgamal?”
Ae amɨn yurɨ kɨnda dakon amɨn da pudaŋ kɨ kabɨ bamot aŋek emat wamjil kaŋ, uŋun amɨn yut tebai dɨma egɨpdaŋ.
Iyɨ dakon gen teban do, “On uŋun Piŋkop dakon gen” yaŋ yaŋek amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgaŋ. Nak gawak namaŋ uŋun koko yo ɨsalɨ asak.’
Uŋudon wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ ak do aŋtɨdok agɨt. Uŋun yum amɨn sotni toŋ kaloŋɨsok dɨ baŋ kɨsitni kwenikon wɨtjɨŋek paŋmɨlɨp agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek meŋi ae datni dɨma paŋpulugosok. Aŋek ji da uŋun amɨn do yaŋ yoŋ, ‘Uŋun amɨn tagɨ asak nido yo uŋun Piŋkop do kɨlɨ manjɨgɨt.’
‘Uŋun dabɨl da yo asat uŋun pɨndakgaŋ mani mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaŋ, ae geno nandaŋ, mani mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaŋ pɨsoŋ. Do Piŋkop da dɨwarɨni wɨrɨrɨk yomjak do but tobɨl ak do dɨma nandaŋ.’ ”
Aŋagek mibɨlɨ yaŋ do aŋakgamaŋ uŋun dakon but pɨso gen yaŋ mandawit, JUDA AMƗN DAKON KƗLA AMƗN MADEP.
Uŋudon gɨn emat amɨn kɨnda Jon dakon busuŋɨ aŋopjak do yabekgɨt. Yabekban uŋun da kɨŋ dam teban yutnon wɨgɨ Jon dakon tegɨ mandaŋ dagagɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek Pita, Jems, ae Jon kɨsi tɨmɨkban kɨwit. Kɨŋ burɨkon jɨgɨ madepsi nandaŋek
Nak gɨldarɨ gɨldarɨ Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan ji gat egek amɨn yoyɨŋ dekgɨm. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak abɨdok do dɨma nandawit? Mani Piŋkop da papiakon nak do gen mandabi uŋun da arɨpmon noman tosak.”
Uŋudon gɨn Yesu da paŋdetni yoyɨŋban boron wɨgek Betsaida kokupmon mibɨl taŋ kɨŋakwa Yesu da amɨn kabɨ madep uŋun yoyɨŋban waseŋ kɨwit.
Mani gen uŋun yawit uŋun kɨsi upbal taŋek gen dakon kosirɨ dɨma pɨsagɨt.
Yaŋban Pita da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn dɨwarɨ dakon nandaŋ gadat wɨtdal kɨsak kaŋ, nak yaŋ arɨpmɨ dɨma abeŋ.”
Amɨn da bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ kɨsit kandapyoni wamgwit, mani uŋun amɨn tebai do nap teban si paŋdagagɨt. Amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma abɨdogɨ.
gɨptɨm kaloŋɨ anjil.’ Gen yaŋ tosok, do amɨn wam da bamorɨ dɨma, gɨptɨm kaloŋɨ amal.
Yaŋ aba Pita da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, nin ɨdon egɨp do tagɨsi nandamaŋ. Nin yut kabeŋ kapbɨ aneŋ. Kɨnda gak do, kɨnda Moses do, ae kɨnda Elaija do aneŋ.”
Jap naŋ yɨgakwa Erodias dakon gwi da paŋabɨŋ ɨŋamnikon kap agɨt. Aban Erot ae amɨn jap nawit uŋun kɨsi da kaŋ galak tawit. Kaŋ galak taŋ Erot da mɨŋat gɨmoŋ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Ni yo do galak tosol uŋun nayɨŋbɨ tagɨ gabeŋ.”
Yesu paŋdetni kapbɨ gat kɨŋ notni kabɨkon altawit. Kɨŋ altaŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep notni paŋgwasɨŋba pɨndakgwit. Ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn dɨwarɨ da apba notni gat gen emat aba pɨndakgwit.
Yaŋ tɨdaŋban amɨn morapmɨ da gen tebai iyɨŋek dɨma yaŋ tɨdosak do iyɨwit. Mani madepsi sigɨn yaŋ tɨdaŋek yagɨt, “Dewit Dakon Monji, bupmɨ nandaŋ nam!”
Amɨn jap yet tɨŋtɨŋosok uŋun Piŋkop gen tɨŋtɨŋosok.
Jon da ɨlɨkba pɨgɨk paŋ egɨpgut uŋun bɨt madep kɨnda mani kamel uŋun dakon daŋgwani baŋ wasaŋbi. Aŋek bɨt gɨp kɨnda bobaŋ napmɨ do wamgut. Japni uŋun pɨlak pɨlak ae kabaŋ kok.
“Gak da gen uŋun yal, uŋun ni bɨsapmon altokdaŋ? Ni yo da mibɨltok altaŋban kaŋek uŋun yo morap altosak dakon bɨsap kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandaneŋ?”
Iyɨŋba Yesu yaŋ yagɨt, “Jiyo kɨsi nandak nandakji mɨni aŋakwan uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaŋ, ma? Yo kɨnda amɨn kwasopgwan pɨgɨsak uŋun da amɨn dakon but arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋupbal asak.
Wɨsa dɨma dagaŋakwan Yesu pɨlisisok pɨdaŋ yut yɨpmaŋek mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon paŋkɨ egek bɨsit pi agɨt.
Kandap gwɨl paŋek agɨpni, aŋek paba pɨgɨk kaloŋɨ gɨn ɨlɨkba pɨgɨsak.
Kokup kɨndakon kɨŋ yut kɨndakon gɨn yɨgek pɨŋ kɨni.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Disikon bret niaŋ da toŋ. Kɨŋ pɨndakgɨt.” Kɨŋ pɨndak abɨŋ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Bret kɨsit kɨnda, ae tap kɨlap bamorɨ yaŋ gɨn taŋ nimaŋ.”
Bɨsap kɨndakon pakbi ɨdap ɨleŋɨkon mɨŋat amɨnyo aeni yoyɨŋ dekgɨt. Amɨn madepsi da abɨŋ uŋudon muwugakwa Yesu boron wɨgɨgɨt. Boron yɨgakwan amɨn morap ɨleŋɨkon yɨkgwit.
Mani kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek nak da kalɨp Galili mɨktɨmon mibɨltaŋ damɨŋek kɨkeŋ.”
Amɨn uŋun kɨsirɨkon da abɨdaŋek yaŋban kokup yɨpmaŋek waŋga pɨgɨgɨmal. Pɨgɨ dabɨlɨkon ɨlɨp sulek kɨsit da wɨtjɨŋ yɨpmaŋek iyɨgɨt, “Yo dɨ pɨndakdal, bo dɨma?”
Yaŋban Pita da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Uwal da gɨgek nakyo kɨsi nɨt do ani kaŋ, gak do wasɨp dɨma yokeŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋban notni kabɨ kɨsi yaŋ gɨn yawit.
Amɨn dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm tɨpmɨ toŋ tɨm yombem, uŋun amɨn Piŋkop gen nandaŋek but galagon da abɨdoŋ.
Aŋakwan Yesu bot buŋɨkon busuŋ kɨdɨŋ kɨndakon wɨtjɨŋek dɨpmɨn pagakwan paŋdetni da aŋyolek iyɨwit, “Yoyɨŋdet, nin pakbi naŋ kɨmotneŋ do nandabɨ yo ɨsalɨ asak?”
Yesu yaŋ aŋek aeni pakbi ɨdap ɨleŋɨkon pɨgɨgɨt. Pɨgakwan amɨn morapmɨ yol aŋaŋ uŋudon kwa Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt.
“Nin ɨlɨkba pɨgɨk garaŋɨ pudaŋkwikon ɨmal dɨwat kalugɨ pakbikon dɨma sugaŋbi kɨnda naŋ bupnom kaŋ, pakbikon sugono ɨmal dɨwat uŋun da garaŋɨ ɨlɨkban pudaŋ kɨ madepsi akdɨsak.
Gak gen teban nandaŋ mudosol, uŋun yaŋ: ‘Amɨn dɨma dapba kɨmotni; mɨŋat eyo kɨlɨ abi ji yumabi dɨma ani; yo kabo dɨma noni; top dɨma yoni; top gen yaŋek amɨn notji yum dogɨn gen pikon dɨma yopni; amɨn dakon yo kabɨ paŋkɨlɨgek dɨma tɨmɨtni; meŋ dat do nandaba wukwanek geni guramɨtni.’ ”
Kɨlɨ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn kɨla amɨn da ɨŋamon agek Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma yoyɨki? On amɨn morap gen yaŋ gaba niaŋ nandaŋ yomɨsal?”
Yaŋ nandaŋek ɨgayɨŋban uŋudon gɨn yawini jɨptaŋban gɨptɨmɨ kɨlek taŋban nandagɨt.
Amɨn Tagɨ da uŋun bɨsap dɨma aŋpɨsɨp asak tam mɨŋat amɨn morap kɨsi pasɨlnom. Mani mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ iyɨ do kɨlɨ manjɨgɨt uŋun do bupmɨ nandaŋek bɨsap aŋpɨsɨp akdɨsak.
Kɨŋ paŋdetni gat Pita gat yaŋ yoyɨni, ‘Uŋun da kalɨp Galili mɨktɨmon mibɨltaŋ damɨŋek kɨk do kɨlɨ dayɨgɨt, do uŋudon kɨŋ koni.’ ”
iyɨŋba Yesu kɨŋ kɨsitnikon abɨdaŋek ɨlɨkban pɨdagɨt. Yaŋ aban sotni yɨpmaŋakwan jap noni do oman agɨt.
Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ da kosiron ɨmalni yalɨwit. Aŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ da kɨŋ kɨndap kɨlɨŋ mandaŋ paŋobɨŋ kosiron yalɨwit
Ae jap yet dɨwarɨ da joŋ kelɨ toŋ tɨmgwan mawit. Uŋun joŋ kelɨ toŋ gat kɨsi kwaŋek wutjɨŋba kɨmak mudawit.
Yaŋ aba Yesu da nawa gen yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji Parisi amɨn gat ae Erot gat uŋun dakon yis do pasalek kaŋ kɨmotni.”
Yaŋ aban kaŋakwa Elaija gat Moses gat altaŋbal Yesu gat gen yaŋ nandat aba pɨndakgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gen uŋun nandaŋek Yesu aŋakba kɨmotjak do kosit wɨsɨwit. Uŋun Yesu do si pasalgwit, nido mɨŋat amɨnyo da Yesu dakon gen yogokni do tamtam yawit.
Jon dam teban yutnon yɨpba yɨgakwan Yesu Galili Provinskon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ Piŋkop dakon Gen Bin Tagɨsi yaŋ teŋteŋaŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Yaŋdo, Parisi amɨn ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nido paŋdetgoni uŋun babɨk dakon gen teban yapmaŋek kɨsirɨ dɨma sugaŋek jap noŋ?”
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Sisaria Pilipai kokup pap uŋun dakon kokup monɨŋ monɨŋ tawit uŋudon kɨwit. Kɨŋek paŋdetni kosiron yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Mɨŋat amɨn da nak do namɨn yaŋ yoŋ?”
“Yesu kalugɨ egakwan kat.” Yaŋ yaŋban gen uŋun do nandaba bamɨ dɨma agɨt.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da yaŋ akdaŋ: peni kɨnda da padɨge uwal da kɨsiron yɨpban aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak, ae amɨn kɨnda da mɨŋat monjɨyoni uwal da kɨsiron yopban dapba kɨmotdaŋ, ae mɨŋat monjɨyo da meŋi datniyo do yaŋ gɨn akdaŋ.
Uŋudeŋ gɨn Sunduk da pudaŋ kɨ kabi bamot aŋek iyɨ emat wamjil kaŋ, amɨn kabɨni tebai dɨma egɨpdaŋ. Yaŋ ani kaŋ pasɨl mudokdaŋ.
Abɨsok mɨŋat amɨnyo ekwaŋ uŋun Piŋkop manji ɨmɨŋek yo yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ aŋ. Uŋun kabɨkon da amɨn kɨnda nak ae geno do mayagɨ nandɨsak kaŋ, Datni dakon tɨlɨmni paŋek telagɨ aŋelo kabɨ gat apni bɨsapmon, Amɨn Dakon Monji da uŋun amɨn do mayagɨ yaŋ gɨn nandakdɨsak.”
Yoba tɨmɨgek amɨn kɨsisi jap arɨpmɨsi nawit.
Kɨlɨ amɨn morapmɨ da Pailaron kɨŋ altaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Bɨlagɨ bɨlagɨ asal, uŋudeŋ gɨn dam tebanon yɨkdak kɨnda pulugaŋ yɨpbɨ kɨsak.”
Yabekbini 12 uŋun dakon mani yaŋ: Saimon (mani kalugɨ Pita yaŋ iyɨgɨt),
Ji yaŋ aŋek babɨkji dakon yaŋ teban tok gen guramɨgek Piŋkop dakon gen maba kɨsak. Ae uŋun gɨn dɨma, yo morap dɨwarɨ kɨsi yaŋ gɨn aŋ.”
Amɨn mibɨltok kɨwit ae buŋon yolgwit kɨsi da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Osana! Piŋkop aŋkɨsino! ‘Piŋkop dakon gɨsamɨ toŋ amɨn uŋun Amɨn Tagɨ da manon abɨsak.’
Mani, namɨn da nak da amɨn tet do yɨtjak, ae namɨn da gwandeŋ tet do yɨtjak uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma yaŋ dagokeŋ. Tamo uŋun Piŋkop da amɨn kɨlɨ manjɨŋ yopgut uŋun dakon gɨn.”
“Nak asisi dayɨsat, Piŋkop da yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ gat ae Piŋkop abɨŋ yɨp do manji gen yogok gat dakon dɨwarɨ tagɨ wɨrɨrɨtjak.
ae Andru, Pilip, Batolomiu, Matyu, Tomas, Jems Alpius dakon monji, Tadius, Saimon Selot,
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk ɨmni. Amɨn kɨnda nak dakon man yaŋek wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ asak uŋun amɨn nikon da nak do yaŋba yokwi tok asak? Uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma.
Yaŋ yaŋban gɨkwem da pɨŋ ɨlɨmɨk yomaŋakwan gen kɨnda uŋungwan da yaŋ altagɨt, “Uŋun Monjɨno, nak uŋun do but dasi galak taŋ ɨmɨsat. Ji geni nandani.”
Aŋakwa Yesu da amɨn dɨma yoyɨni do yaŋsop tebaisi aŋyomgut. Aŋek mɨŋatjok jap ɨmɨŋba nosak do yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋban Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep tɨmtɨm yaŋek apba pɨndagek koŋ tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Koŋ, gen kaga ae mɨrak sopsop amɨn, gak monjɨ on yɨpmaŋdet! Wagɨl kɨŋek buŋon on monjɨgwan dɨmasi pɨgɨki!”
Gen uŋun nandaŋek nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt. Mani Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Monjɨnoni, amɨn Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan pɨgɨk do aŋtɨdok aŋ.
Iyɨŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Monjɨsok mɨŋat pak do aŋ uŋun bɨsapmon notni gat jap kelek tagɨ egɨpni? Dɨma. Monjɨsok egakwan jap kelek arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ.
Yaŋba Yesu da gen uŋun nandagɨt, mani dɨma nandabi wup agɨt. Aŋek kɨla amɨn yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Dɨma pasolgi. Ɨsal nandaŋ gadat aki.”
Uŋun kɨsit kɨlda kɨnda, Maria dakon monji. Padɨk padɨkni uŋun Jems, Josep, Judas ae Saimon. Ae samɨni binapninon ekwaŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋek ɨŋtaŋ ɨmɨŋek nandaba pɨŋban ɨmgwit.
Amɨn kabɨ madep kɨŋakwa iyɨ dakon paŋdetni 12 kabɨ gat ae amɨn dɨwarɨ gat da tɨlak gen dakon mibɨlɨ nandak do iyɨwit.
Nido but nandak nandak nikon dɨma pɨgɨsak, ɨsal kwasopnikon pɨgakwan uŋun da aŋkosit aŋakwan kosirɨ naŋ abɨgɨsak.” (Yesu yaŋ yagɨt, do jap kɨsisi Piŋkop da dabɨlon kɨlegɨ gɨn.)
Yaŋban Jon da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, nin kaŋapno amɨn kɨnda da gak da manon koŋ yolban kamaŋ. Mani nin da kabɨkon nani kɨnda dɨma, do yaŋsop aŋ ɨmɨmaŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn da paŋkewalni do kaŋ kɨmotni.
Yoyɨŋban but galak nandaŋek moneŋ ɨmni do yaŋ teban tawit. Judas uŋun nandaŋek Yesu kɨsitnikon yɨpjak dakon kosit wɨsɨgɨt.
Jems gat Jon gat, Sebedi dakon monjɨ bamot, uŋun da Yesukon altaŋ ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨmal, “Yoyɨŋdet, nit yo kɨnda do gayɨkdamak, uŋun gak da abi do nandamak.”
Aŋakwan mɨŋat dɨwarɨ dubagɨsogon da agek pɨndak nandaŋyo awit. Uŋun mɨŋat kabɨkon kɨnda mani Maria, kokupni Makdala, ae Maria ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda uŋun Jems buŋon nani gat Josep gat dakon meŋi, ae Salome gat kɨsi akgwit.
Yesu da tɨmɨsok dɨ kɨŋek Jems, Sebedi dakon monji gat padɨge Jon gat pɨndakgɨt. Uŋun bamot boron yɨgek tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨkni bɨsawɨk paŋmɨlɨp aŋyo aŋakwal pɨndakgɨt.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Kapaneam kokupmon kɨwit. Kɨŋ altaŋek Sabat bɨsapmon Yesu da Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgek Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt.
Yesu Ɨleŋ Olipmon yɨgakwan Telagɨ Yut Madep ason tet tagɨt. Aŋakwan Pita, Jems, Jon ae Andru da iyɨ gɨn Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit,
Yaŋ iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn mɨragɨ pɨsagɨt, ae melɨ tagap taŋek gen kɨlegɨsi yagɨt.
Yesu Kristo, Piŋkop dakon Monji, uŋun dakon Gen Bin Tagɨsi ɨdon da wasosok.
Yo uŋun Amɨn Tagɨ da agɨt, aŋakwan nin da kono yo masɨ masɨmɨsi asak.’ ”
Gɨldat 6 mudaŋakwa Yesu da Pita, Jems, ae Jon yoyɨŋban buŋon yolba ɨleŋ dubagɨ kɨndakon wɨgɨwit. Ɨleŋon iyɨ gɨn egek kaŋakwa Yesu dakon gɨptɨm kulabɨk aŋek ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ da yawit, “Uŋun Elaija.” Ae dɨwarɨ da yawit, “Uŋun kombɨ amɨn kɨnda, kombɨ amɨn kalɨp egɨpgwit uŋuden amɨn kɨnda.”
Mɨktɨm kɨnda dakon amɨn da pɨdaŋba mɨktɨm kɨnda dakon amɨn gat emat wamdaŋ. Ae kɨla amɨn madep kɨnda dakon amɨn da pɨdaŋba kɨla amɨn madep kɨnda dakon amɨn gat emat wamdaŋ. Aŋakwa mɨktɨm dɨwarɨkon wudɨp akdɨsak, ae mɨktɨm dɨwarɨkon amɨn da jap do madepsi aŋek dɨwarɨ da kɨmotdaŋ. Mɨŋat monjɨ kwapmɨ toŋ da monjɨ altok do aŋek sugaŋba tepmɨ nandaŋ, uŋudeŋ gɨn uŋun yo morap altoni bɨsapmon, bɨsap madep kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandani.
Mandaŋ dagaŋban Yesu da obip amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nak do kabo noknok kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋek emat agak sɨba ae kɨndap kɨrɨŋ tɨmɨgek nak abɨdok do abeŋ, ma?
Don yabekbi kabɨ da abɨŋ Yesu aŋgwasɨŋek yo awit ae Piŋkop gen yawit uŋun dakon geni iyɨwit.
Paŋdetni 10 kabɨ gen uŋun nandaŋek Jems gat Jon gat do butjap nandawit.
Yaŋ nandaŋakwa yoyɨgɨt, “Ji wurɨpdagek dɨma pasolni. Yesu Nasaret kokupmon nani tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakbi uŋun kok do abeŋ. Uŋun kɨlɨ pɨdaŋ kɨk, ɨdon mɨni. Tamoni oni kabɨt.
Aŋek yutnon wɨgek amɨn yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido kunam kugɨyo madepsi aŋ? Mɨŋatjok uŋun dɨma kuŋwak, uŋun ɨsal dɨpmɨn pokdok.”
Piŋkop dakon gen guramɨkgaŋ amɨn uŋun nak dakon meŋno ae padɨk padɨkno ae samɨno kabɨ.”
do yoyɨŋbɨ amɨn kabɨ madep kokup monɨŋ monɨŋ ae kokup terɨ dɨŋgwan kɨŋek jap yumaŋ noni.”
Gen yaŋ yagɨt: “Amɨn kɨnda nak da manjikon apdɨsak. Uŋun dakon tapmɨm da nak dakon tapmɨm yapmaŋdak. Nak oman monjɨni dakon pɨŋbinisi egɨsat, do kandap gwɨlni dakon nap pabɨŋ yɨgek tagɨ dɨma wɨtdalgeŋ.
Altaŋ ɨban kɨŋ Yesu dakon paŋdet kabɨni kunam takba pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Ae Yesu da tɨlak gen kɨnda yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda da wain pini aŋek nagal agɨt. Aŋek uŋun nagalon wain sop bamaŋ tɨl do gapma kɨnda wayɨkgɨt. Aŋek kɨla amɨn da kabo noknok pɨndat do yut dubak kɨnda wɨtjɨŋban wɨgɨgɨt. Yut wɨtjɨŋek kɨla amɨn da pini aŋek bamɨ pakpak bɨsapmon bamɨ dɨ namni yaŋ nandaŋek wain pi uŋun da kɨsiron yɨpmaŋek mɨktɨm dubagɨkon kɨgɨt.
amɨn akgwit en da pɨndagek yawit, “Nibaŋ ak do aŋek on donki bɨlagɨ wɨtdalgamal?”
Gen yaŋ yoyɨŋakwan meŋi padɨk padɨkni da abɨŋ yomakon agek Yesu yomakon pɨsak do gen yɨpba wɨgɨgɨt.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda Gerasa amɨn da mɨktɨmon kɨwit.
Aŋek topmon da man madep ɨmɨŋ mudaŋek ɨmal gami ɨlɨgek iyɨ dakon pabɨ pɨgɨk paŋ ɨmgwit. Paŋ ɨmɨŋek tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotjak do ɨlɨk aŋaŋ kɨwit.
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma yagɨt. Yaŋ aban kaŋek Pailat nandaban ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek yaŋ teban tok gen kɨnda yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo nido nayɨki, tagɨ gabeŋ. Mɨktɨmno terɨ kɨnda pɨdaŋ gak do tagɨ gabeŋ.”
Jap naŋ yɨgakwa Yesu da bret kɨnda abɨdaŋ, Piŋkop ya yaŋ iyɨŋek, pudaŋ paŋdetni do yomgut. Yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Tɨmɨgek noni, on nak dakon gɨptɨm tɨmno.”
Aŋakwan uŋudon gɨn koŋni toŋ amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ yagɨt,
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo amɨn but nandak nandagon da wɨŋ waŋga kwaŋ uŋun da amɨn dakon but paŋupbal aŋ.
yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Butno jɨk taŋakwan kɨmot kɨmotno noman taŋ naban nandɨsat. Do ji ɨdon Piŋkop do nandaŋek egɨpni.”
Yaŋ tɨdaŋban Yesu da nandaŋek kosiron agek yaŋ yagɨt, “Iyɨŋba apban.” Yaŋban amɨn da dabɨlɨ mɨni amɨn yaŋ iyɨwit, “But galak nandaŋek pɨda. Opbi do yosok.”
Yesu da Galili Pakbi Ɨdap kɨdɨpmɨŋ kɨŋek Saimon gat padɨge Andru gat pɨndakgɨt. Uŋun amɨn bamot tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨkni pakbi ɨdapmon mabal pɨgakwan egɨpgumal. Pini uŋun tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl do pi agak amɨn bamot.
Pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo Yesu gat paŋdetni 12 kabɨ gat uŋun yutnon opgwit.
Yaŋba Yesu da paŋdet kabɨni pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn iyɨ arɨpmɨ dɨma ani, mani Piŋkop da arɨpmɨ tagɨ asak. Piŋkop da yo morap ak do tagɨ asak.”
Yaŋ kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋek tɨmtɨm yaŋek kokupmɨ kokupmɨ kɨŋ yoyɨŋba sotni toŋ amɨn wayɨk wamaŋek Yesu dukwan dukwan egɨpgut uŋudon paŋkɨwit.
Yaŋban Yesu da mibɨlni amɨn dɨmasi yoyɨni do yoyɨgɨt.
Aŋakwa Yesu uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek, kokupnikon kɨŋakwan paŋdetni yolgwit.
Yaŋ aba ji nak nolgaŋ do aŋek amɨn kɨsi morap da ji do butjap nandakdaŋ. Mani tebai agek egɨ wɨgakwa bɨsap madepmon wɨgɨsak amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da yokwikon baŋ tɨmɨtdɨsak.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon mɨŋat monjɨ kwapni toŋ, ae mɨŋat monjɨ mum noŋ uŋun bupmɨsi.
Aŋakwan emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn da Yesu ɨŋamɨkon kɨmakban kaŋek yagɨt, “On amɨn asisi Piŋkop dakon Monji egɨpgut.”
Yaŋ aŋakwa Sadyusi amɨn dɨwarɨ da Yesukon apgwit. (Uŋun amɨn kabɨ amɨn kɨmakbi arɨpmɨ dɨma pɨdoni yaŋ nandaŋ.) Abɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit,
Wamaŋ ɨmɨŋek top iyɨŋek yaŋ yawit, “Gɨldat tagɨ, Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn madep!”
Mani amɨn morapmɨ da uŋudon kwaŋ yaŋ pɨndak nandaŋyo awit. Yaŋ nandaŋek kokup morapni yopmaŋ yopmaŋ aŋek amɨn morapmɨ mɨktɨm kosit tɨmtɨm yaŋek uŋun da kalɨp kɨŋ altawit.
Pɨndagek uŋudon gɨn yaŋ yoban nandaŋek datni Sebedi gat pi amɨni gat boron si yɨgakwa Yesu yolgɨmal.
Yaŋban Yesu da kaŋ galak taŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yo kaloŋɨ tosok uŋun dɨma asal. Gak kɨŋ yo morapgo yumaŋ naŋek uŋun dakon moneŋ baŋ yoni mɨni amɨn do yobi. Yaŋ aŋaki yo tagɨsi Kwen Kokupmon taŋ gamdɨsak. Yaŋ aŋek abɨŋ nak nol.”
Aŋek si aŋpulugosak do madepsi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gwano kɨmotdɨsak, do abɨŋek kɨsitgo da wɨtjɨŋbɨ kɨlek taŋek egɨpjak.”
Aŋakwa Yesu da yoyɨŋ degek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da dayɨŋdet aŋ uŋun do pɨndak kɨmotni. Uŋun amɨn ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkni dubagɨ paŋek mɨŋat amɨnyo da makeron ‘gɨldat tagɨ’ yaŋ yoyɨni yaŋ do galak toŋ.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo jɨgɨ dakon bɨsap mudaŋakwan ‘gɨldat dabɨl pɨlɨn tuk akdɨsak, ae kanek dɨma teŋteŋokdɨsak.
Ae gɨk kundu yɨpmaŋek mokdaŋ, aŋakwa kwen kundukon yo tebai toŋ uŋun da kwakwalɨtdaŋ.’
Mɨktɨm da iyɨ upmagakwan gɨgɨ wɨŋ tamɨ yopmaŋek bamɨ toŋ.
Yaŋba Pailat da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn madep naŋ yɨpbo kɨsak do nandaŋ?”
Uŋun da yaŋ yagɨt, nido Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Koŋ gak on amɨn yɨpmaŋ degek wɨŋ kɨ!”
Uŋun bɨsapmon Parisi amɨn da abɨŋ Yesu aŋkewal do aŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak da wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda abɨ kaŋek nin da gandano Piŋkop da gak yabekban pɨl da pini asal yaŋ gandaneŋ.”
Gen dayɨsat uŋun amɨn morap kɨsi do yosot. Kaŋ kɨmotni.”
Yaŋ aban kaŋek Yesu tebai abɨdawit.
Wɨsa dagokdo Yesu gat paŋdetni gat kosiron kɨwit. Kɨŋek pik kɨndap uŋun kɨlɨ wagɨlsi kɨbɨdagɨt kawit.
Mani uŋun dakon aŋpak uŋun jikon dɨma tosak. Jikon da amɨn kɨnda amɨn tagɨ man pak do nandɨsak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn oman amɨnji egek amɨn tagɨ man pasak.
Yaŋ yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Ji sigɨn dɨma nandaba pɨsosok, ma?”
Uŋun do nak yaŋ dayɨsat, ni yo kɨnda do Piŋkop bɨsit iyɨŋek yo uŋun tɨmɨtni do nandaŋ gadaŋ kɨmotni kaŋ, yaŋ gɨn tɨmɨtdaŋ.
Opban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak ninaŋ aŋgabeŋ do nandɨsal?” Yaŋban dabɨlɨ mɨni amɨn da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, nak sɨŋtok do nandɨsat.”
Aŋakwan wuda wamak morapmɨ da aŋpulugok do pi aŋtɨdok aŋakwa tepmɨ madepsi nandaŋek egɨpgut. Wuda wamak yumaŋ nok do aŋek moneŋni kɨsi yomɨŋ mudagɨt. Aban sotni dɨma tagap tagɨt, si madep tagɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek aeni wain kɨnam abɨdaŋek, Piŋkop ya yaŋ iyɨŋek, yoban kɨsi da nawit.
Yaŋban Pita da wasɨp yaŋek yagɨt, “Gak da gen uŋun yosol nak dɨma nandɨsat.” Yaŋ yaŋek nagalon da wigat mibɨlon pɨgɨgɨt.
Kundu gat mɨktɨm gat pasɨldamal, mani nak dakon gen uŋun dɨmasi pasɨldɨsak.”
Kɨŋek kosiron yaŋ nandat aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Namɨn da tɨp kɨnam dakon tɨp madep aŋtobɨlban pɨsosak?”
Maria Makdala kokupmon nani gat ae Maria Josep dakon meŋi gat da kaŋakwal Yesu dakon bumjotni yɨpgut.
Yaŋ aŋakwa but tebani do butjap nandagɨt. Aŋek butni yokwi taŋban kobok tobɨl tobɨl aŋek pɨndagek amɨn kɨsirɨ gɨreŋɨkbi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Kɨsitgo aŋnɨŋnɨŋ a.” Yaŋban amɨn uŋun kɨsirɨ aŋnɨŋnɨŋ aban kɨlek tagɨt.
Wɨsawɨsa do mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae kɨla amɨn ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae gen kokwin amɨn kabɨ morap gat da muwugek gen kɨnda aŋteban awit. Aŋek Yesu nap teban naŋ wamaŋ ɨlɨk aŋaŋ Pailat da kɨsiron aŋkɨ yɨpgwit.
Gen uŋun yaŋ teŋteŋaŋban Pita da Yesu abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ ɨleŋɨkon agek tebai iyɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni da kɨŋek amɨn but tobɨl ani do yoyɨwit.
Jit da tagapmɨ, amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi yaŋ iyɨkdo, ‘Dɨwarɨgo wɨrɨrɨk gamɨsat’, bo uŋudeŋ iyɨkdo, ‘Pɨdaŋ yalɨŋ potgo tɨmɨgek pɨlɨk bamok aki’?
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ nandani do tɨlak gen kɨnda gat dayɨko nandani. Amɨn kɨnda jap yet pigaga tɨŋtɨŋosok.
Aŋakwa pabɨŋ yɨgek paŋdetni 12 kabɨ yoyɨŋban apba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda mibɨltok amɨn ak do nandɨsak kaŋ, buŋonsi agek amɨn morap dakon oman amɨn egɨpjak.”
Yesukon altaŋek ɨmalni ɨlɨk donki bɨlagɨ da kwenon yopmaŋakwal Yesu pawɨgɨ uŋudon yɨkgɨt.
Ae kandapgo da yokwi aki do gayɨŋban kaŋ, kandapgo mandaŋ dagoki. Gwɨnɨmbɨl egek Tɨpdomon kɨndap tebanon pɨgɨki yaŋ do kandapgo mandaŋ dagaŋek tagapmɨ egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni do amɨn aki.
Aŋek uŋudon da kɨŋek Liwai, Alpius dakon monji, takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt yutnikon yɨgakwan kagɨt. Kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Abɨŋ nak nol.” Yaŋban Liwai pɨdaŋek Yesu yolgɨt.
Yaŋba Pailat da amɨn dakon burɨ moni do Barabas pulugaŋ yɨpban mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyokon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋakwan emat amɨn yoyɨŋban Yesu baljawit. Aba don tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakba kɨmotjak do yoyɨgɨt.
Amɨn uŋun amɨn da kɨsitni ae kandapmɨyo nap teban naŋ wamwamɨ dakon arɨp dɨma agɨt.
Kɨmakbi da pɨdoni bɨsapmon mɨŋat eyo agak dɨma tokdɨsak. Aŋelo Kwen Kokup ɨsal ekwaŋ uŋun da tɨlagon egɨpdaŋ.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek koŋ morapmɨ yol yomɨŋek sot amɨn morapmɨ bɨt nelak soŋ yoba kɨlek tawit.
Mani mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep burɨ sugaŋek yaŋ yoyɨwit, “Ji Pailat da Barabas naŋ yɨpban kɨsak do iyɨni.” Yaŋ yoyɨŋba amɨn da yaŋ gɨn iyɨwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo yokwisi amɨn paŋupbal ak kɨnda don dɨma toktogɨ tamokon akban kokdaŋ.” (On gen manjɨsak amɨn da pakyaŋsi nandɨsak.) “Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn Judia mɨktɨmon egɨpni uŋun pasal kabapgwan tepmɨsi wɨgɨni.
Ae mɨŋat kɨnda da eni yɨpmaŋek kɨŋ wɨli kalugɨ pasak kaŋ, uŋun mɨŋat yumabi asak.”
Yaŋ aŋek pik kɨndap kɨnda dubagɨkon da tam dɨrɨm kagɨt. Yaŋ kaŋek bamɨ dɨ toŋ bo dɨma yaŋ do kapmatjok da kɨŋ wɨsɨgɨt. Mani bamɨ dɨ dɨma pɨndakgɨt. Tamɨ gɨn pɨndakgɨt, nido pik kɨndap dakon bamɨ toktok bɨsap dɨma.
Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun yaŋ gɨn kɨlɨ agɨt. Amɨn da oman aŋɨmni do dɨma pɨgɨt. Iyɨ mɨŋat amɨn morap paŋpulugokdo, ae iyɨ dakon gɨptɨmnaŋ paregek yumaŋ naŋ yop do pɨgɨt.”
Mɨktɨm amɨn da arɨpmɨ dɨma egɨpmɨ tɨmon amɨn kɨnda da yaŋ tɨdaŋek yosok, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ dakon kosit aŋdɨmdɨm ani, kositni pasɨŋ aŋmɨlɨp ani.’ ”
Dabɨlɨ kɨlek taŋban Yesu da yabegek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak kokupmon dɨma kɨki, yutgokon kɨki.”
Yoni mɨni amɨn ji gat bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ egɨpdaŋ, do tagɨ paŋpulugoni. Mani nak ji gat bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ dɨma egɨpdamaŋ.
Yaŋban amɨn uŋun yaŋ yagɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, nak monɨŋɨsogon da gen teban morap guramɨk aŋ aŋ opgum da obɨsat.”
“On mɨŋat amɨn kabɨyo nin gat gɨldat kapbɨ ekwamaŋ. Kɨlɨ japni kɨsi naŋ mudaŋ, do bupmɨ nandaŋ yomɨsat.
Yaŋba aŋtobɨlek yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da kombɨ amɨn Aisaia dakon nandak nandakni aŋtagap aban jamba but amɨn ji do gen yaŋ mandagɨt: ‘Uŋun amɨn kabɨ gen kaga dagɨn nak man madep namaŋ, mani but dasi nak dɨma nandaŋ namaŋ.
Aban Yesu uŋun tapmɨmni abɨkwa nandaŋek tobɨlek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkno namɨn da ɨgayɨsak?”
Yaŋ yaŋba Pita da tebaisi yaŋek yagɨt, “Asisi dayɨsat, amɨn uŋun yoŋ nak dɨmasi nandaŋ ɨmɨsat. Top yosot kaŋ, jobɨt tagɨ tɨmɨkgeŋ.”
Uŋun da aŋelo kabɨni yabekban kɨŋ amɨn iyɨ do manjɨkbi kabɨ mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ ekwaŋ uŋun paŋmuwutdaŋ.”
Aŋakwan paŋdetni mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ kɨŋ Piŋkop dakon geni yoyɨŋ aŋaŋ kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Amɨn Tagɨ uŋun gat egek paŋpulugaŋakwan wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ aŋek geni joŋɨk paŋteban agɨt.
Aŋteban aŋek bot yɨpmaŋek pɨgakwa uŋudon gɨn mɨŋat amɨnyo da Yesu kaŋ nandaŋyo awit.
Bɨsap morapmɨ koŋ da aŋakgo kɨmotjak yaŋ nandaŋek maban kɨndapmon ae pakbikon pɨgɨgɨt. Tapmɨm taŋ gamɨsak kaŋ, nit do bupmɨ nandaŋek paŋpulugoki.”
Yerɨ dɨwarɨ da mɨktɨm tɨpmɨ toŋ tɨmon mawit. Uŋun kwenjok tawit, do tepmɨ kwawit, mani tɨp kwenon mɨktɨm morapmɨ dɨma, do gelɨ tagɨ dɨma yopba kɨwit. Do gɨldat da wɨŋ pɨndakban alek tawit.
Jon da gen yaŋ yaŋban Erodias da Jon do nandaban yokwi taŋban aŋakba kɨmotjak do si nandagɨt. Mani arɨpmɨ dɨma,
Yɨgakwan amɨn da “Yesu Nasaret amɨn obɨsak” yaŋ yaŋba nandaŋek gen madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yagɨt, “Yesu, Dewit Dakon Monji, bupmɨ nandaŋ nam!”
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da paŋdetni bamorɨ yabegek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kokupmon kɨŋ kaŋbal amɨn kɨnda pakbi kwoba kɨnda guramɨk apban jil gat domdom akdaŋ. Jil uŋun amɨn naŋ yol aŋkɨnjil.
Amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ ‘Nak Kristo’ yaŋ yokdaŋ. Ae dɨwarɨ da ‘Nak kombɨ amɨn kɨnda’ yaŋ yokdaŋ. Yaŋ yaŋek wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ akdaŋ. Aŋek mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ Piŋkop da iyɨ do kɨlɨ manjɨkbi uŋun paŋkɨlɨkba kosit kɨlegɨ yɨpmaŋ detni do pini madep akdaŋ. Mani arɨpmɨ dɨma akdaŋ.
Aŋakwan Jon dakon paŋdetni gen bini nandaŋek kɨŋ bumjotni abɨdaŋ aŋkɨ tɨp kɨnamon yɨpgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋek yawit, “Telagɨ bɨsap madepmon dɨma abɨdoneŋ. Yaŋ aneŋ kaŋ, mɨŋat amɨnyokon pɨdok pɨdok noman tokdɨsak.”
Kaŋbal yut kɨndakon wɨkwan kaŋ, uŋun yut dakon ami yaŋ iyɨnjil, ‘Yoyɨŋdetnit da yosok, “Nak gat paŋdetnoni gat da Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap noneŋ dakon yut burɨ dukwan tosok?” ’
Moses da kalɨp yaŋ mandagɨt: ‘Ji meŋ datyo dakon pɨŋbi egek geni guramɨtni’, ae ‘Amɨn kɨnda da meŋ datyo do gen yokwi kɨnda yosak kaŋ, uŋun amɨn si aŋakba kɨmotjak.’
Ɨleŋ Olipmon wɨgakwa Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda tosok uŋun da arɨpmon ji manji namdaŋ. Gen uŋun yaŋ: ‘Sipsip dakon kɨla amɨn aŋakgo kɨmagakwan sipsip waseŋ kɨ iyɨ iyɨ kɨkdaŋ.’
Mani aeni wasɨp yaŋek yagɨt, “Dɨma.” Tɨmɨsok dɨ egek amɨn kapmatjok akgwit uŋun da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gak asi Yesu da kabɨkon nani kɨnda. Gak Galili amɨn kɨnda.”
Yesu dakon man bin ɨreŋ taŋban kɨla amɨn madep Erot uŋun kɨsi da nandagɨt. Amɨn dɨwarɨ da Yesu do yaŋ yawit, “Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn uŋun kɨmoron da pɨdagɨt, aŋek wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ agak dakon tapmɨm taŋ ɨmɨsak” yaŋ yawit.
Bɨlagɨ bɨlagɨ Yapyap Bɨlak bɨsapmon wasok kɨnda yaŋ awit: Juda mɨŋat amɨnyo da dam tebanon yɨkdak amɨn kɨnda dakon man yaŋakwa, Pailat da yopban kɨŋ kɨŋ awit.
“Dapmaŋakwa kaloŋɨ kɨnda egɨpgut uŋun iyɨ dakon monji. Monji uŋun do galagɨsi nandagɨt. Buŋon iyɨ dakon monji yabegek yaŋ nandagɨt, ‘Monjɨno kwan kɨla amɨn da uŋun do nandaba wukwanek geni nandaŋek bamɨ dɨ ɨmni.’
Sabat kɨndakon Yesu gat paŋdetni gat uŋun wit pi kaga kɨndakon kɨwit. Kɨŋek paŋdetni da wit bamɨ dɨwarɨ jɨmɨk dagawit.
Yaŋba Yesu da gen yoyɨgɨt uŋudeŋ gɨn yoyɨgɨmal. Abal nandaŋ yomɨŋakwa donki aŋkɨgɨmal.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨsal, do kɨlek taŋek kɨki.” Yaŋ iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn dabɨlɨ sɨŋtaŋek Yesu yolgɨt.
Kɨlɨ Yesu Tair kokup yɨpmaŋek Saidon kokup kɨŋ yapmaŋek Dekapolis mɨktɨm uŋun kɨsi yapmaŋek Galili Pakbi Ɨdap uŋudon kɨgɨt.
Aŋakwa binapnikon mɨŋat kɨnda akgɨt, uŋun dagaŋ mok aŋek yawini maŋakwa egakwan bɨlak 12 agɨt.
Kalɨp Erot da padɨge Pilip dakon mɨŋatni Erodias tuwɨl pagɨt. Aban Jon da Erot yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak gen teban yapmaŋek padɨgɨgo dakon mɨŋatni tuwɨl pal. Uŋun tagɨ dɨma.” Gen uŋun nandaŋek Erot da obip amɨni yabekban kɨŋ Jon abɨdaŋek nap teban naŋ wamaŋ dam tebanon yɨpgwit.
Yaŋ iyɨŋbal uŋun amɨn da yut madep kɨnda kwen nani do dolɨsak. Uŋun yutnon jap noknok tamo ae amɨn yɨyɨt tamo kɨlɨ paŋnoman abi da toŋ. Uŋudon japnin paŋkosit anjil.”
Yesu gɨldat dɨ egɨ aeni Kapaneam kokupmon kɨŋek yutnikon wɨgakwan kokup amɨn da abapni dakon gen nandawit.
Ɨleŋon da tobɨl pɨŋek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Yo uŋun pɨndakgaŋ uŋun dakon gen amɨn kɨnda dɨmasi iyɨni. Aŋakwa Amɨn Dakon Monji kɨmoron da pɨdosak, uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn tagɨ yoyɨni.”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban gen uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaba pɨsagɨt ae iyɨk do si pasalgwit.
Yesu gen yaŋakwan uŋudon gɨn paŋdetni 12 kabɨkon da kɨnda mani Judas altaŋ yomgut. Amɨn kabɨ madep emat agak sɨbani ae kɨndap kɨrɨŋni tɨmɨgek buŋon yolgwit. Mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn ae kɨla amɨn uŋun da yabekba apgwit.
Amɨn da Yesu burɨkon koŋ kɨnda egɨsak yaŋ yawit uŋun do aŋek gen uŋun yagɨt.
Kɨŋek paŋdet kabɨni ɨŋtaŋek bret dɨwarɨ dɨma paŋkɨwit, bret kaloŋɨ kɨnda da gɨn boron tagɨt.
Asi, Piŋkop da papiakon gen mandabi uŋun da arɨpmon Amɨn Dakon Monji kɨmot akdɨsak. Mani Amɨn Dakon Monji uwal da kɨsiron yɨpjak amɨn, awa! Uŋun amɨn meŋi da dɨma aŋalagɨt tam tagɨ.”
Koŋ da bɨsap morapmɨ yaŋ asak. Monjɨno tebai abɨdaŋek maban mɨktɨmon maŋ pagek tarak kwakwagɨ da gen kaganikon pawɨŋ tɨmɨkdak, aŋakwan geni wamtɨmsisak, ae gɨptɨmɨ kɨsisi kɨtɨraŋ kɨsak. Nak paŋdetgoni koŋ yolni do yoyɨko aŋtɨdok aŋ, uŋun da arɨpmɨ dɨmasi yolyolɨ.”
“Amɨn kɨnda nak do nandaŋek amɨn monɨŋ oden kɨnda but da abɨdosak kaŋ, uŋun nak naŋ abɨdosok. Ae amɨn kɨnda nak abɨdosak kaŋ, uŋun nak naŋ gɨn dɨma abɨdosok, Datno nak yabekban pɨgɨm uŋun naŋ abɨdosok.”
Nandaŋek morapmɨsi da yutnon muwuk tugaŋek dɨwarɨ yomakon yɨk tugaŋba Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨgɨt.
Kɨŋakwan Yesu da paŋdetni pɨndagek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Yoni morapmɨ amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak da kagagwan pɨgɨk do aŋtɨdok aŋ.”
Obɨŋ jap noknok tamokon jap naŋ yɨgek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, jikon da kɨnda da nak uwalno da kɨsiron nepdɨsak. Uŋun amɨn nin gat yɨgek jap nomaŋ.”
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji gen emat nido aŋ?”
Mani Yesu da uŋun jamba but amɨn yaŋ nandaŋ yomɨŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido nak aŋkewalgaŋ? Moneŋ tabɨlɨ kɨnda aŋabɨŋ naba koko.”
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdet morapni yɨpmaŋek pasal kɨŋ mudawit.
Ji Amɨn Tagɨ Piŋkopji uŋun but gat, ae wup gat, ae tapmɨmgo gat, ae nandak nandakgo gat kɨsi but dasi galak taŋ ɨbi.’
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da aeni dabɨlɨkon kɨsirɨ wɨtjɨgɨt. Yaŋ aban dabɨlɨ wagɨl kɨlek taŋban yo morap tagɨ pɨndakgɨt.
Parisi amɨn ae Juda amɨn kɨsisi babɨkni dakon gen teban yolek kɨsirɨ sugaŋek gɨn jap naŋ naŋ aŋ.
Yesu gen yaŋ iyɨŋakwan, muwut muwut yutni dakon kɨla amɨn Jairus da yutnon da amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ Jairus yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gwago kɨlɨ kuŋwak, uŋun do nido yoyɨŋdet ɨsal dogɨn jɨgɨ ɨmɨsal?”
Yesu da uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Tair kokupmon kɨgɨt. Kɨŋ yut kɨndakon wɨgek pasɨlɨ egek yɨk yawot akeŋ yaŋ nandagɨt, mani pasɨlɨ egɨp do aŋtɨdok agɨt.
Aŋakwan Kwen Kokupgwan da gen kɨnda yaŋ altagɨt: “Gak Monjɨno. Butdasi galak taŋ gamɨsat. Butno gak do tagɨsi asak.”
Gen kɨnda saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Namɨn da lam koleŋek kwoba naŋ gap asak, bo pɨgat kagagwan yɨpjak? Dɨmasi, tamonikon yɨpno teŋteŋosok.
Uŋun do Piŋkop da mɨŋat wɨli kɨlɨ paŋmuwukgɨt, do amɨn da dɨma paŋwasekdo.”
“Nin da nandaŋapno Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, ‘Nak da Telagɨ Yut Madep amɨn da awit uŋun tuwɨlek gɨldat kapbɨ da butgwan yut ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda abeŋ. Yut uŋun amɨn kɨsit da agagɨ dakon tɨlak dɨma abeŋ.’ ”
Amɨn da yubam tam, moneŋ madepsi tɨmɨk yoni mɨni amɨn do yomnom.” Yaŋ yaŋek mɨŋat uŋun gen tebai iyɨwit.
Yaŋ nandaŋek egakwa Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kombɨ amɨn kɨnda man bini mɨktɨm dɨwarɨkon toŋ, mani iyɨ da kokupmon yawi dɨwatni gat ae yutnikon amɨn gat da mani dɨma aŋenokgoŋ.”
tamoni do Piŋkop da yo madepsi ɨmdɨsak. Mɨktɨmon egɨpjak bɨsapmon yo morap kalɨp yopmaŋ dekgɨt uŋun dakon tɨlak yapmaŋek yo morapmɨ ɨmdɨsak. Uŋun amɨn da yutni, peni padɨk padɨkyo, sami, meŋi, mɨŋat monjɨyo ae mɨktɨm morapmɨsi tɨmɨtdɨsak. Mani uŋun gɨn dɨma, amɨn da yo yokwi aŋyomdaŋ. Yaŋ aŋakwa bɨsap madep apjak bɨsapmon egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokdɨsak.
Wɨli 7 kabɨ kɨsi da pawit, do amɨn da kɨmoron da pɨdoni bɨsap madepmon namɨn dakon mɨŋatni asak?”
Aŋek dabɨni uŋun bini nandaŋek “Burɨ upbal tak” yaŋ yaŋek yutnikon iyɨŋ aŋaŋ kɨk do apgwit.
Yaŋ yopban kaŋek Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ paŋmuwugek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, on sakwabat uŋun da paret yopmaŋdak uŋun da amɨn morap da yopmaŋ si yapmaŋdak.
Kɨŋ mudaŋakwa monjɨsok kɨnda ɨmalni kwakwagɨ kɨndanaŋ gɨn ɨmegek Yesu yolgɨt. Emat amɨn da uŋun monjɨsok kɨsi abɨdok do awit,
Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋakwan pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo paŋdetni da abɨŋ Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Mɨktɨm amɨn dɨma ekwaŋon ekwamaŋ, ae gɨldat kɨlɨ pɨgɨkdɨsak,
Amɨn Piŋkop gen nandaŋek butni dɨma pɨsoŋ uŋun jap yet kosiron mawit uŋuden. Sunduk da abɨŋ gen tagɨ butnikon toŋ uŋun gwayeŋ paŋkɨsak.
Aba amɨn dɨwarɨ da pɨdaŋ Yesu do top sɨtnok gen yaŋ yawit,
Yo kɨnda amɨn kwasopgwan pɨgɨsak uŋun da amɨn dakon but arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋupbal asak. Yo kɨnda amɨn butgwan da wɨŋ waŋga kɨsak uŋun da amɨn dakon but aŋupbal asak.”
“Yoyɨŋdet, Moses da gen kɨnda yaŋ mandagɨt, ‘Amɨn kɨnda monjɨ mɨni da kɨmagakwan mɨŋatni ɨsal egɨpjak kaŋ, padɨge da paŋakwan monjɨ paŋalasak.’
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Mibɨlɨ nido? Ni gulusuŋ naŋ agɨt?” Yaŋban mibɨltok yawit si yapmaŋek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakbɨ kɨmotjak!”
Mani dɨsi Moses dakon gen maba kwanek yaŋ yoŋ, ‘Amɨn kɨnda da meŋi bo datni yaŋ iyɨsak, “Nak yo on kɨlɨ Piŋkop do manjɨgɨm. Dɨma tam tagɨ paŋpulugokom.” ’
Aŋakwan Judia mɨktɨmon ae Jerusalem kokup papmon egɨpgwit amɨn Jonon kɨwit. Yokwini yaŋkwok aŋakwa Jodan Pakbikon telagɨ pakbi soŋ yomgut.
Kɨlɨ Yesu pakbi ɨdap yɨpmaŋek ɨleŋ kɨndakon wɨgɨgɨt. Wɨgek yabekbini dagoni do nandagɨt amɨn yoyɨŋban iyɨkon abɨŋ muwukgwit.
Nido Yesu da mɨŋat amɨnyo do bret kokwinɨk yomgut uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandawit. But nandak nandakni dɨma pɨsaŋakwan egɨpgwit.
Yaŋba Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep yoyɨŋban mɨktɨmon yɨkgwit. Yɨgakwa bret 7 kabɨ tɨmɨgek Piŋkop ya yaŋ iyɨŋek paŋdetni da kokwinɨk yomni do yomgut. Yoban mɨŋat amɨnyo do yomgwit.
Uŋuden gɨn notni dɨwarɨ kɨsi mɨŋat uŋun paŋek monji mɨni da kɨmakgwit. Kɨmagakwa mɨŋat uŋun don kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Moses da ni gen teban naŋ damgut?”
Yaŋban yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakbɨ kɨmotjak!”
Yaŋba Yesu da burɨ yokwi taŋban yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Mɨŋat monjɨ yopba nagon apgut. Dɨma kɨrɨŋɨk yomni. Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun amɨn mɨŋat monjɨyo da tɨlagon ekwaŋ uŋuden amɨn dakon.
Mani wasok wasogɨkon Piŋkop da amɨn wasaŋek ‘mɨŋat ae wɨliyo kɨsi wasagɨt.’
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat aeni Jerusalem kɨŋ altawit. Aŋek Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan pɨgɨ agɨpgut. Agakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ, ae gen teban dakon yoyɨŋdet amɨn, ae kɨla amɨn Yesukon opgwit. Obɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit,
Uŋun bɨsapmon paŋdetni 12 kabɨkon kɨnda egɨpgut mani Judas Iskariot. Uŋun da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨkon kɨŋek Yesu kɨsitnikon yɨpjak do yoyɨgɨt.
Iyɨŋba nandaŋek Yesu da amɨn kadɨm uŋun abɨdaŋban amɨn kabɨ madep yopmaŋek ɨleŋɨkon kɨgɨmal. Kɨŋ Yesu da kɨsitni amɨn uŋun da mɨragon yɨpban pɨgɨgɨt. Aŋek kɨsitnikon ɨlɨp sulek melɨkon wɨtjɨgɨt.
Altaŋ yoban tobɨl kɨŋ notni dɨwarɨ yoyɨŋbal nandaba bamɨ dɨma agɨt.
Tap gat kɨndap gat amɨn kɨsikon altosak.
Mibɨlni yaŋ teŋteŋaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gwano, nandaŋ gadatgo da gak aŋkɨlek ak. Uŋun do butgo yaworɨ taŋakwan kɨki. Sotgo kɨlɨ pasɨlak.”
Nak dakon gen nandaŋek burɨkon yɨpmaŋdak uŋun amɨn Piŋkop da saŋbeŋek nandak nandak ɨmdɨsak. Mani geno nandaŋek burɨkon dɨma yɨpmaŋdak uŋun amɨn geno dɨwarɨ nandagɨt uŋun pasɨl ɨmdaŋ.”
Mɨktɨm kɨnda dakon amɨn da pudaŋ kabɨ bamorɨ aŋek emat wamjil kaŋ, uŋun mɨktɨm tebai dɨma tokdɨsak.
Mɨktɨm uŋun da ɨleŋon bɨt kabɨ madep jap naŋek egɨpgwit.
Yaŋ nandaŋek madepsi pasalek yaŋ tɨdawit. Mani uŋudon gɨn Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji teban taŋek atni. Nak naga obɨsat. Dɨma pasolni.”
Yaŋban iyɨgɨmal, “Tagɨ pandeŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋbal Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Uŋun asi, tepmɨ pakdɨsat uŋun pakdamal.
Amɨn kɨŋ ap awit uŋun da yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmɨŋek wunda kwalkwal aŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Ae! Gak Telagɨ Yut Madep tuwɨlek gɨldat kapbɨ da butgwan kaluk ak do yagɨl,
Tap uŋun yo galagɨsi. Mani tap dakon galagɨ pasɨljak kaŋ, niaŋsi aŋek galagɨni aŋkaluk aneŋ? Ji tap yombem egek notji gat but kaloŋsi egɨpni.”
Yaŋ yaŋban Yesu da iyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi gayɨsat, abɨsok kalbi pup kosit bamot dɨma yaŋakwan gak da nak do wasɨp kosit kapbɨ yokdɨsal.”
Nak amɨn 5 tausen do bret 5 kabɨ pɨdaŋ yomgum bɨsapmon, ji jap dɨwat yɨk madepsi niaŋ da sɨmɨlba tugawit?” Yaŋban yaŋ iyɨwit, “Yɨk madepsi 12 kabɨ.”
‘Uŋun do aŋek wɨli da meŋi datniyo yopmaŋek mɨŋatni gat muwukbal
Yaŋban uŋudon gɨn mɨŋatjok pɨdaŋek kɨŋ ap aban kaŋek yaŋ kɨmakgwit. (Mɨŋatjok bɨlakni 12 kabɨ.)
Gɨldat bamorɨ egek don Yapyap Bɨlak ae Bret Yisni Mɨni Dakon Jap Noknok Bɨsap Madep altok do aŋakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da muwugek yaŋ yawit, “Niaŋ aŋek Yesu aŋkewalek abɨdaŋ aŋatno kɨmotjak?”
On amɨn Kristo, asi Juda amɨn dakon Kɨla Amɨn Madepni kaŋ, tɨlak kɨndapmon da pɨŋban kaŋek nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmneŋ.” Uŋudeŋ gɨn kabo noknok bamot terɨ terɨ dapbi uŋunyo kɨsi yaŋba yokwi tok aŋ ɨmgumal.
Amɨn da ji tɨmɨk paŋpaŋ gen pikon depni bɨsapmon dɨma pasolni. Ni gen baŋ yoyɨneŋ yaŋ dɨma nandani. Uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop da ni gen dayɨsak uŋun baŋ yoyɨni. Yaŋ aŋakwa ji dakon gen dɨma asak, uŋun Telagɨ Wup dakon gen asak.
Uŋun yutnon Saimon yopmi gɨptɨmɨ kɨndapmɨ soŋakwan sot aŋek pakgɨt. Uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ
Yesu Jerusalem kɨŋ altaŋek Telagɨ Yut Madep uŋun da nagalgwan pɨgɨgɨt. Pɨgɨ yo morap pɨndak aŋ aŋ kɨgɨt, mani gɨldat pɨgɨk do aŋakwan paŋdetni 12 kabɨ gat tobɨlek Betani kokupmon kɨwit.
Yoyɨŋakwan amɨn kabɨ kɨnda apgwiron da amɨn 4 kabɨ da amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi kɨnda wamaŋ uŋudon aŋapgwit.
“Nandani! Amɨn kɨnda da jap yet tɨŋtɨŋok do pigaga kɨgɨt.
Muwugakwa Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut dakon kɨla amɨn kɨnda mani Jairus, uŋun da abɨŋ Yesu kaŋek burɨkon kɨŋek gawak ɨmgut.
Yesu Sonda wɨsa dagokdo kɨmoron da pɨdaŋek mibɨltok Maria Makdala kokupmon nani altaŋ ɨmgut. (Uŋun mɨŋat Yesu da kalɨp koŋ 7 kabɨ burɨgwan egɨpgwit baŋ yol ɨmgut.)
Yaŋba Yesu da nandaŋek yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn sotni mɨni uŋun wuda wamagon dɨma kwaŋ. Amɨn sotni toŋ uŋun dagɨn wuda wamagon kwaŋ. Nak amɨn kɨlegɨ yaŋ ɨlɨt do dɨma opgum, yokwi pakpak yaŋ ɨlɨt do opgum.”
Tebaisi iyɨŋban kɨrɨŋɨk ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak yutgokon kɨŋ Amɨn Tagɨ da gak do bupmɨ nandaŋek wasok madep ak uŋun dakon gen bin yawi dɨwat kabɨgo yoyɨŋ mudoki.”
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “12 kabɨ jikon kɨnda nak gat bret ɨdapmon sɨbɨŋek nomak uŋun.
Yaŋ yaŋek Galili Provinskon dukwan dukwan kɨsi agek Juda amɨn dakon muwut muwut yut morapmon Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋek koŋ yol yomɨŋek agɨpgut.
Mɨŋat uŋun gɨptɨmɨkon wasok noman tagɨt uŋun nandaŋek burɨ sugaŋban nɨmnɨmɨgek Yesu da buron gawak ɨmɨŋek mibɨlni yaŋ teŋteŋagɨt.
Iyɨŋba yagɨt, “Disi jap yoba noni.” Yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn morapmɨsi ekwaŋ, do moneŋ 200 danari baŋ jap yumneŋ kaŋ arɨpmɨ asak. Yaŋ aneŋ do yosol, ma?”
Kɨŋakwa mɨrɨm madep aŋek pakbi tamalɨgakwan boron pɨgɨwit. Pɨgɨ tugaŋban bot pakbigwan pɨgɨk do agɨt.
mani nandak nandakni mɨktɨm dakon yo morap do nandaŋ, ae moneŋ paŋmuwut dakon galaktok da Piŋkop gen wɨtjɨŋba bamɨ dɨma tosok.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji Piŋkop dakon gen teban yum pɨndagek dɨsi dakon yaŋ teban tok gen guramɨkgaŋ.
Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yagɨt, “Ji Piŋkop nandaŋ gadaŋ ɨmni.
Kalbi dɨpmɨn pokdok ae gɨldat kalba waŋga waŋga agakwan jap yet kwoŋ. Mani niaŋsi aŋek kwoŋ uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandɨsak.
Gen uŋun yaŋek aeni saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Gen on nandak do galak toŋ amɨn ji pakyaŋsi nandaŋek mibɨlɨ nandaŋ pɨsoni.”
Pɨdaŋ agakwan mɨŋat amɨnyo yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Sabat bɨsap dakon gen teban da yokwi aneŋ do yosok? Bo tagɨ aneŋ do yosok? Amɨn paŋmɨlɨp aneŋ do yosok, bo dapba kɨmotni do yosok?” Yaŋban gen tamoni dɨma iyɨwit.
Meŋi yaŋ yaŋban mɨŋat gɨmoŋ uŋun tepmɨ wɨgek Erot yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn dakon busuŋɨ abɨsok gɨn ɨdapmon yɨpmaŋ nabi.”
Bamɨ taŋakwa pi ami da bamɨ pasak.”
Ji Piŋkop dakon gen teban yɨpmaŋek babɨkji dakon gen paŋteban aŋek paŋ ekwaŋ.”
Yaŋban uŋudon gɨn amɨn morapmɨ da dabɨlon yalɨŋ potni tɨmɨgek abɨgɨgɨt. Yaŋ aŋakwan amɨn kawit uŋun da tamtam yaŋek Piŋkop aŋkɨsiŋek yawit, “Yo kalugɨsi altaŋban komaŋ!”
Mani Yesu da yoyɨŋban opba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nandaŋ, Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ dakon amɨn tagɨ da iyɨ do nandaba wukwanek pi madepsi amɨn do yoba aŋ. Ae geni guramɨk kɨmotni do nandaŋ.
Yaŋban mɨŋat gɨmoŋ uŋun da waŋga kɨŋ meŋi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Ni yo naŋ namjak do iyɨkeŋ?” Yaŋban iyɨgɨt, “Kɨŋ Jon Telagɨ Pakbi Sogok Amɨn uŋun dakon busuŋɨ uŋun do iyɨki.”
Mandaŋ dagaŋ ɨdapmon yɨpmaŋ aŋabɨŋ mɨŋatjok uŋun do ɨban aŋkɨ meŋi do ɨmgut.
Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “On yut madep pɨndakdal, uŋun dakon tɨp notni da kwenon dɨma taŋ taŋ akdaŋ. Tuwɨlba kɨsisi maŋ mudokdaŋ.”
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji kaŋba tapmɨmni ae tɨlɨmni gat gɨkwemon da apban kokdaŋ.
“Uŋun bɨsapmon ji dɨsi do kɨla ani. Amɨn da gen pikon depdaŋ ae Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon pawɨgɨ nap kɨrɨŋbaŋ baljokdaŋ. Ji nak nandaŋ namaŋ do amɨn da ji paŋkɨ mɨktɨm dakon kɨla amɨn madep da ɨŋamon depba atdaŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon nak dakon gen yoyɨni.
Aŋakwan Yesu Liwai da yutnon kwan yɨgek jap nawit. Moneŋ tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn ae yokwi pakpak amɨn morapmɨ Yesu gat paŋdetni gat jap nawit. (Uŋuden amɨn morapmɨsi da Yesu yolgwit.)
Yaŋ aba kɨnda gat yabekban kwan aŋakba kɨmakgɨt. Yaŋ aba pi monjɨ morapmɨ yabekgɨt. Dɨwarɨ si baljaŋek dɨwarɨ dapba kɨmakgwit.
“Nak gayɨsat, pɨdaŋ yalɨŋ potgo tɨmɨgek yutgokon kɨ.”
Yesu aeni bɨsap kɨnda gat Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgek amɨn kɨnda kɨsirɨ gɨreŋɨkbi kɨnda yɨkban kagɨt.
Muwugek paŋdet kabɨnikon da dɨwarɨ kɨsitni dɨma sugaŋek jap ɨsal tɨmɨk naŋyo aba pɨndakgwit.
Aŋakwan Saimon gat notni kabɨ gat Yesu wɨsɨŋek apgwit.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat telagɨ yut madep dakon nagal yɨpmaŋ waŋga pɨŋakwa monjɨ kɨnda da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, tɨp madepsi baŋ yut tagɨsisi dɨ awit do dɨgo pɨndat!”
Amɨn kɨnda da ‘Nido yaŋ amal’ yaŋ dayɨŋban kaŋ yaŋ iyɨnjil, ‘Amɨn Tagɨ da pi kɨnda ak do aŋek yosok. Donjok yɨpban opdɨsak.’ ”
Judas uŋudon gɨn Yesukon kɨŋ altaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet!” Yaŋ iyɨŋek mogɨmɨkon mandaŋ nagɨt.
Aŋek yaŋ tɨdaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yesu, Piŋkop Wɨkwisi dakon Monji, gak niaŋsi aŋnam do abɨsal? Piŋkop da manon tepmɨ pi dɨma nabi do yaŋ teban ta.”
Naŋakwa Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “On yawino. Amɨn morapmɨ gat saŋbek saŋbek ak do parekdat.
Yaŋ aba pi ami da aeni oman monjɨ kɨnda yabekdak. Uŋun pi monjɨ busuŋɨkon aŋagek yo yokwisi aŋɨmgwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon emat wuwɨk gat ae dubagɨkon emat aŋ uŋun dakon gen bin apba nandaŋek butji dɨma pasolni. Uŋun yo morap altokdaŋ, mani mɨktɨm da mudosak bɨsap madep kɨlɨ uŋun yaŋ dɨma nandani.
Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madepmon wɨgek paret yopyop tamo da kapmatjok yɨkgɨt. Yɨgek pɨndagakwan amɨn morapmɨ da paret yopgwit. Moneŋ morapmɨ taŋ yomgwit amɨn uŋun da moneŋ madep yopgwit.
Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon da pɨŋek uŋudon gɨn Jems gat Jon gat tɨmɨkban, Saimon gat Andru gat uŋun da yutnon wɨgɨwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu da wasaŋek paŋdetni yoyɨŋ degek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji da tepmɨ madepsi pakdɨsak. Aŋakwan kɨla amɨn, ae mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn, ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat da manji ɨmɨŋek aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Kɨmagek gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Uŋun nak mani. Ji don kaŋakwa Amɨn Dakon Monji Tapmɨm Ami da amɨnsi tet do yɨkban kokdaŋ. Aŋek kaŋakwa Kwen Kokup dakon gɨkwemon da apban kokdaŋ.”
“Ma, amɨn on ni gen naŋ yosok? On Piŋkop kulabɨsak on! Namɨn amɨn da dɨwarɨ wɨrɨrɨt pi asak? Uŋun pi Piŋkop dagɨn agagɨ!”
Yaŋ iyɨŋban uŋudon gɨn wudani kɨbɨdaŋakwa gɨptɨmni kɨlek tagɨt.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak nido nak do amɨn tagɨsi yaŋ nayɨsal? Piŋkop kaloŋɨ gɨn uŋun amɨn tagɨsi.
Sabat bɨsap mudaŋakwan pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo Maria Makdala kokupmon nani, ae Maria Jems dakon meŋi, ae Salome, uŋun mɨŋat kapbɨ da bɨt nelak, ae yo mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ kɨbaŋɨ tagɨsi, Yesu dakon bumjotni soŋ ɨm do yumaŋ paŋkosit awit.
Yesukon abɨŋek amɨn koŋni morapmɨ gat egɨpgut uŋun burɨ pɨsagɨt ae ɨlɨkba pɨgɨkni toŋ da yɨkban kawit. Yaŋ yɨkban kaŋ pasalgwit.
Uŋun mɨŋat Israel mɨŋat kɨnda dɨma, uŋun Grik mɨŋat kɨnda Ponisia tetgɨn Siria mɨktɨmon altagɨt. Yesu da gwi dakon koŋ yol ɨmjak do bɨsit tebai iyɨgɨt.
Amɨn kɨnda mɨktɨm dakon yo morap kɨsi paŋ egakwan egɨp egɨpni pasɨl ɨmjak kaŋ, uŋun yo morap da arɨpmɨ dɨma aŋpulugoni. Egɨp egɨpni uŋun yo kɨnda naŋ arɨpmɨ dɨma yumjak, wagɨlsi pasɨl ɨmjak.
Iyɨŋba Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Gen uŋun bamɨ yoŋ. Elaija kɨlɨ abɨŋ yo morap paŋmɨlɨp agɨt. Aŋakwan amɨn da galaktokni yolek yo mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ Piŋkop da papiakon gen tosok uŋun da tɨlagon aŋ ɨmgwit. Mani Piŋkop da papiakon gen kɨnda mandabi uŋun yaŋ: ‘Amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji manji ɨmɨŋek yo yokwi madepsi aŋ ɨmdaŋ.’ Uŋun gen mibɨlɨ nido tosok?”
Aŋek yutnon awɨgɨ Yesu da buron yɨpdo aŋek amɨnon kwa tɨdaŋba yut kwenon awɨgɨwit. Awɨgek Yesu da si yɨkgɨt da kwenon yut tuwɨlba kosit pɨsaŋakwan uŋudon da amɨn uŋun wayɨgon pagakwan nap aŋyawot aŋakwa pɨgɨgɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋban monjɨ uŋun Yesukon aŋopgwit. Aŋopba koŋ da Yesu kaŋek uŋudon gɨn monjɨ maban mɨktɨmon pagek tobɨl tobɨl aŋek tarak kwakwagɨ da gen kaganikon pawɨŋ tɨmɨkgɨt.
Mani Erot uŋun nandaŋek yagɨt, “Kalɨp nak da Jon dakon tegɨ mandaŋ dagagɨm, uŋun amɨn dasi kɨmoron da pɨdagɨt.”
Yaŋ kaŋek Pita da Yesu da gen yagɨt uŋun nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, ka! Apma pik kɨndap yokwi tosak do yagɨl abɨsok oni kɨbɨdak!”
Pɨlɨn pɨlɨndo bot pakbi ɨdap binapmon taŋakwan Yesu iyɨ gɨn tap kɨdɨpmɨŋon egɨpgut.
Gen uŋun nandaŋ mudaŋek Yesu mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋ kɨsak do tebai iyɨwit.
Aban Yesu da wasok agɨt uŋun dakon gen bin amɨn dɨma yoyɨni do yaŋsop aŋyomgut. Mani amɨn da geni dɨma nandaŋek yaŋba madepsi ɨreŋ tagɨt.
yaŋ yagɨt, “Nin abɨsok Jerusalem kɨŋapno amɨn da Amɨn Dakon Monji mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn uŋun da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ. Yaŋ aŋek gen pikon yɨpmaŋek kɨmotjak do yaŋ dagok akdaŋ. Yaŋ dagok aŋek Amɨn Ŋwakŋwarɨ Kabɨ da kɨsiron yɨpdaŋ.
“Gak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ amɨn dɨma yoyɨki. Aŋek mukwa sogok amɨnon kɨŋek gɨptɨmgo yolɨki. Aŋek Moses da yagɨt uŋun da tɨlagon paret aŋaki amɨn da asi kɨlek tal yaŋ gandani.”
Kɨŋ mɨktɨm tɨm kɨnda mani Golgata uŋudon altawit. (Golgata uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ uŋun Busuŋ Kɨdat Ɨleŋ.)
Kɨŋ kɨla amɨn da yomakon altaŋek amɨn da upbalap madep ae gen kunamyo aŋakwa pɨndak nandaŋyo agɨt.
Yaŋban uŋun mɨŋat amɨn kabɨkon da amɨn kɨnda da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, monjɨno koŋ da burɨkon yɨgek gen yogok kositni sopmaŋdak, do gagon aŋobɨsat.
Aban Josep da kɨŋ ɨmal kwakwagɨ kɨnda yumaŋ aŋabɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjot tɨlak kɨndapmon naŋ abɨŋ uŋun ɨmal naŋ wamgut. Wamaŋ aŋkɨ tɨp kɨnam kɨndakon yɨpmaŋek tɨp madepsi kɨnda aŋtobɨlban abɨŋ yoma sopgut.
Yaŋ yaŋakwa man bini da tepmɨsi ɨreŋ taŋek Galili Provins arɨpmɨsi agɨt.
Tap kɨlap monɨŋ monɨŋ kaloŋ kaloŋ kɨsi taŋ yomgwit. Uŋun kɨsi gɨsamɨgek paŋdetni da kokwinɨk yomni do yomgut.
Iyɨŋba yagɨt, “Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni dakon gen pasɨlɨ uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ ji baŋ dayɨŋ teŋteŋosot. Mani Piŋkop dɨma nandaŋ ɨmɨŋek waŋga ekwaŋ amɨn tɨlak gen gɨn nandaŋ.
Iyɨŋban emat amɨn 100 dakon kɨla amɨn da yaŋ yagɨt, “Asi kuŋwak.” Yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek Josep da bumjot aŋkɨsak do yaŋ mudaŋ ɨmgut.
Mani ‘Amɨn da yabekgɨt’ yaŋ iyɨneŋ kaŋ, uŋun kɨsi tagɨ dɨma asak, nido amɨn morapmɨ da Jon do kombɨ amɨn bamɨsi kɨnda yaŋ nandaŋ. Do Jon dakon man bin aŋupbal aneŋ kaŋ nindapdaŋ.” Yaŋ do si pasalek
Yo mɨŋat da agagɨ kɨlɨ aban dagak. Nak kɨmokgo gapmakon nepni do uŋun mɨŋat da pakbi kɨbaŋɨ toŋ naŋ kɨlɨ soŋ namɨk.
Asisi, bɨt madepsi kamel uŋun da ɨmal bupbup da kosit gwagagon arɨpmɨ dɨma pɨgɨgɨ asak. Mani uŋun yapmaŋek yoni morapmɨ amɨn uŋun Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun da kagagwan arɨpmɨ dɨmasi pɨgɨgɨ asak.”
“Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Akdɨsak uŋun dakon bɨsap kwaŋ tosok. Uŋun do ji but tobɨl aŋek Gen Bin Tagɨsi uŋun do nandaŋ gadani.”
Yaŋ yaŋek monjɨ uŋun aŋakba kɨmakgɨt. Kɨmakban bumjotni pigaga naŋ maba waŋga kɨgɨt.
Aban pakbikon da wɨŋek wɨŋek Yesu yaŋ kagɨt: Kundu wɨtdal kɨŋakwan Telagɨ Wup kɨnarɨm da mɨktɨmon paŋ uŋun da tɨlak iyɨkon pɨgɨt.
Parisi amɨn gat gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn gat Jerusalem kokup papmon da obɨŋ Yesu aŋgwasɨŋek muwukgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋba burɨ yokwi taŋban yaŋba kɨk aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Apmiap amɨn ekwaŋ nido wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda kok do yoŋ? Nak asisi dayɨsat, wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ kɨnda dɨma koni, dɨmasi.”
Yaŋ yaŋban yum kaŋek kɨŋ gen bin yaŋ aŋɨreŋ agɨt. Uŋun do aŋek Yesu kokup papmon noman kɨsak do nandaban tɨdok tagɨt. Kokup ɨleŋɨ ɨleŋɨkon gɨn agakwan amɨn morap dukwan dukwan egɨpgwit Yesukon apgwit.
amɨn wam kɨlɨ abi da yumabi aŋpak, pɨndak galaktok, aŋpak yokwi mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ, top gen yogok, kwen wɨgɨk, tagɨsi ekwaŋ amɨn do nandaba yokwi tok nandak nandak, ae not do yokwi yogok, gen kɨrɨŋɨt, ae ŋugɨgɨ aŋpak.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Yo morap altokdɨsak uŋun dakon bɨsap amɨn kɨnda da dɨma nandɨsak. Kwen Kokup aŋeloyo dɨma nandaŋ, ae Monjɨyo kɨsi dɨma nandɨsak. Dat da iyɨ gɨn nandɨsak.
Obɨŋ Pita kɨndap alɨŋek ekwan kagɨt. Mɨŋat uŋun da pakyaŋsi yɨpban kwan kaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Yesu Nasaret kokupmon nani gat kɨsi egɨpgumal.”
Kɨmagakwan Telagɨ Yut Madep dakon yoma ɨmal uŋun kwen da sulugɨ pɨŋ mibɨlɨkon dagaŋ kɨ tɨmɨ bamorɨ agɨt.
ae Jems, Sebedi dakon monji, ae Jems dakon padɨge Jon (uŋun bamot mani Boanages yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ Kɨrɨrɨŋ Amɨn),
Amɨn madepsi apgwit do Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn morapmɨsi do gɨtni gɨtni aba kaŋ bot kɨnda aŋnoman aba nak uŋudon mɨlkaŋ wɨgɨkeŋ.”
Aŋakwan uŋudon gɨn Parisi amɨn kɨŋek Erot dakon amɨn kabɨ uŋun gat muwugek “Niaŋ aŋek aŋatneŋ?” yaŋ do gen paŋkosit awit.
Yaŋban uŋun gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet, tagɨsi yosol. Uŋun asisi, Piŋkop uŋun kaloŋ dagɨn egɨsak, ae Piŋkop kɨnda dɨma egɨsak.
Aŋakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ gat ae gen kokwin amɨn kɨsi morap gat da yaŋ nandawit, amɨn dɨ yaŋ yomno abɨŋ Yesu top gen yaŋ ɨmɨŋek gulusuŋ agɨt yaŋ yaŋakwa aŋatno kɨmotjak yaŋ nandawit, mani Yesu suŋ kɨnda dɨma agɨt yaŋ kawit.
Yaŋban Yesu da aŋtobɨlek iyɨgɨt, “Mango namɨn?” Yaŋ iyɨŋban yagɨt, “Nak mano Amɨn Kabɨ Madep. Nin morapmɨ da ekwamaŋ.”
Yaŋban uŋudon gɨn tap kɨlap sɨmɨl sɨmɨl yɨkni yopmaŋek Yesu yolgɨmal.
Yaŋ aŋek Yesu yut kɨndakon wɨgakwan paŋdetni da iyɨ gɨn egek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nido koŋ uŋun nin da yol do aŋtɨdok amaŋ?”
Yaŋ yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨŋban paŋdetni da amɨn kɨsisi kosirɨ kosirɨ joŋ tɨmon yɨtni do yoyɨwit.
Ae maket tamokon da tobɨlek obɨŋ yaŋ gɨn kɨsirɨ sugaŋek jap noŋ. Uŋun gɨn dɨma, gen teban morapmɨ yolek kap, kwoba, ɨdapyo kɨsi sugoŋ.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak jibaŋ gen kɨnda dayɨkdɨsat. Dayɨko kobogɨ nayɨni kaŋ, nakyo kɨsi kobogɨ tagɨ dayɨkeŋ.
Yesu Galili mɨktɨmon egɨpgut bɨsapmon uŋun mɨŋat kabɨ da yol awɨlek oman aŋ ɨmɨŋek egɨpgwit. Uŋun dagɨn dɨma, ae mɨŋat dɨwarɨ kɨsi Yesu gat Jerusalem kokup papmon kɨwit uŋun kɨsi kaŋakwa Yesu kɨmakgɨt.
Yaŋ aŋek amɨn Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan yoni tɨmɨgek kɨŋ ap dɨma ani do yaŋsop aŋyomgut.
Kosiron kɨŋ amɨn kɨnda kokup pap kɨk do apban kawit, mani Saimon. Uŋun Sairini kokupmon nani kɨnda, Aleksanda gat Rupas gat dakon datni. Emat amɨn da Saimon gen tebai iyɨŋba Yesu dakon tɨlak kɨndapni guramɨkban kɨwit.
Kɨŋakwa koŋ uŋun Yesu kaŋek mɨktɨmon gawagek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek yawit, “Gak Piŋkop dakon Monji.”
Boron da pɨŋakwan, amɨn kɨnda koŋni toŋ uŋun da amɨn kɨmakba paŋkɨ tɨp kɨnamgwan yopmaŋgaŋ mɨktɨmon da abɨŋ altaŋ ɨmgut.
Yesu do gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin dɨma nandamaŋ.” Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nakyo kɨsi namɨn da pi uŋun abeŋ do yaŋ mudaŋ namgut da pi asat uŋun dɨma dayɨkeŋ.”
Uŋun pɨlɨn kaga ae gɨldat kalba amɨn kɨmakba yopmaŋgaŋ mɨktɨmon ae kabapmon egek madepsi yaŋ tɨdaŋek gɨptɨmɨ tɨpbaŋ mandagɨt.
Kɨmakban uŋun da buŋon nani da sakwabat paŋek yaŋ gɨn monji mɨni egɨ kɨmakgɨt. Ae uŋun da buŋon nani yaŋ gɨn agɨt.
“Mani kɨla amɨn da monjɨ kaŋek notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, ‘Amɨn on da egɨ don datni dakon yo morap tɨmɨtdɨsak, do nin amɨn on aŋagek wain pini nin do aŋawatneŋ.’
Buŋon paŋdetni bamorɨ da kokup kɨndakon kɨk do kɨŋakwal Yesu da gɨptɨmɨ kulabɨk aŋek altaŋ yoban amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ kɨnda yaŋ kagɨmal.
Yo pasɨlɨ toŋ ae yo wɨtjɨŋbi da toŋ uŋun kɨsi teŋteŋɨkon tokdaŋ.
Sabat dakon tagaptok bɨsap Neŋgo pɨlɨndo Josep Arimatea kokupmon nani da apgut. Uŋun gen kokwin amɨn kabɨ dakon kɨla amɨn egɨpgut. Amɨn morapmɨ da nandaba wukwan ɨmgwit. Ae uŋun Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Akdɨsak uŋun do jomjom aŋek egɨpgut. Josep uŋun pasol pasolɨ mɨni Pailaron kɨŋ Yesu dakon bumjotni abɨdok do iyɨgɨt.
Dewit Telagɨ Wup da aŋpulugaŋban iyɨ yaŋ yagɨt: ‘Piŋkop da nak dakon Amɨn Tagɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak abɨŋ nak da amɨnsi tet do yɨkbɨ don uwalgo kandap gɨbaŋgogwan yopbo gengo guramɨtni.” ’
Yaŋban Pita da Yesu gen kɨnda yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nin yo morap yopmaŋek gak naŋ gɨn gol awɨlgamaŋ.”
Amɨn Tagɨ Yesu gen uŋun yoyɨŋ mudaŋakwan Piŋkop da aŋenakban Kwen Kokup wɨgɨgɨt da Piŋkop da amɨnsi tet do yɨkdak.
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Kapaneam kokupmon kɨŋ pɨsaŋek yutnon wɨgek Yesu da paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Kosiron ji ni gen naŋ yaŋ?”
Aeni kɨŋ bɨsit aŋ tobɨl abɨŋ paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji dɨpmɨn sigɨn pagek tapmɨm paŋ, ma? Dɨpmɨn arɨpmɨ kwayɨŋ. Bɨsap kɨlɨ abɨk. Amɨn Dakon Monji yokwi pakpak da kɨsiron kɨlɨ uŋun yɨpmaŋgaŋ.
Mani amɨn morapmɨ abɨsok mibɨltok ekwaŋ uŋun da buŋon amɨn akdaŋ. Aŋakwa amɨn morapmɨ abɨsok buŋon ekwaŋ uŋun da mibɨltok amɨn akdaŋ.”
Yɨk mudaŋba bret kɨsit kɨnda ae tap kɨlap bamot uŋun gat tɨmɨgek Kwen Kokup sɨŋtaŋek gɨsamɨkgɨt. Gɨsamɨgek bret jokgal paŋdetni do yoban uŋun da amɨn do kokwinɨk yomgwit. Ae tap kɨlap yaŋ gɨn kokwinɨk paŋdetni do yoban uŋun da amɨn do yomgwit.
Paŋkɨ egek Sabat bɨsapmon Juda amɨn da muwut muwut yutnon wɨgɨ Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt. Aŋakwan amɨn morapmɨ Piŋkop dakon gen nandaŋek yɨkgwit amɨn uŋun tamtam yaŋek yaŋ yawit, “Yo uŋun dukon tɨmɨkgɨt? Nandaŋ kokwin tagɨsi gat ae wasok tapmɨmɨ toŋ agak uŋun namɨnon tɨmɨkgɨt?
Yaŋ yaŋban yutnon wɨgek paŋdetni da uŋun gen dakon mibɨlɨ nandak do iyɨwit.
Kosiron gen emat aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Nin kabɨkon namɨn da mibɨltok amɨn asak?” Yaŋ yawit, do gen kobogɨ iyɨk do mayak tawit.
Yaŋbal yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Niaŋ abeŋ do nandamal?”
Yaŋ yoyɨŋban mɨŋat kapbɨ uŋun pasal nɨmnɨmɨgek tɨp kɨnamon da wɨŋ tɨmtɨm yaŋek kɨwit. Kɨŋ pasol pasol aŋek amɨn dɨ dɨma yoyɨwit.
Aŋek tɨlak kɨndapmon aŋakgwit. Aŋagek ɨmalni tɨmɨt do satu wasok awit.
Mɨŋat amɨn jap naŋba arɨpmɨ aŋakwa jap dɨwat tawit uŋun paŋdetni da yɨk madepsi 7 yaŋ sɨmɨlba tugawit.
Yaŋbal Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Jil gen uŋun yomal uŋun dɨma nandaŋ pɨsaŋek yomal. Nak da tepmɨ madep pakdɨsat uŋun tagɨ panjil?”
Muwugek Yesu do paba pɨgɨk gami kɨnda paŋ ɨmgwit. Yaŋ aŋek nap kelɨ toŋ kɨnda naŋ kɨla amɨn madep dakon pelɨt yombem kɨnda wasaŋek busuŋɨkon wamaŋ ɨmgwit.
Gen on nandak do galak toŋ amɨn ji pakyaŋsi nandaŋek mibɨlɨ nandaŋ pɨsoni.”
Yaŋba Yesu da nandaŋ yoban koŋ da amɨnon da wɨŋek bɨt da butgwan pɨgɨwit. Pɨgakwa bɨt uŋun pasal abɨgɨŋek pakbi ɨdap tagɨt uŋungwan pɨgek kɨmakgwit. Bɨt kaloŋɨsok dɨma, 2 tausen da kɨmakgwit.
Yɨpba Pailat da Yesu yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gak Juda amɨn dakon kɨla amɨn madep, ma?” Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ yagɨt, “Yosol uŋun mani.”
Ɨgayɨŋek yaŋ nandagɨt, “Ɨlɨkba pɨgɨknikon ɨgayɨkeŋ kaŋ, kɨlek tokeŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek boron wɨgek mɨktɨm amɨn da dɨma ekwaŋ tɨmon kɨwit.
ae Judas Iskariot (uŋun egɨ don Yesu uwalni da kɨsiron yɨpgut).
Mani Yesu da tobɨl paŋdetni pɨndagek Pita gen tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Sunduk, gak nepmaŋ det. Gak Piŋkop dakon nandak nandak dɨma yoldal, amɨn dakon nandak nandak yoldal.”
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Jerusalem kokup papmon wɨgɨk do aŋek Yesu iyɨ mibɨltok aŋyoban kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa paŋdetni da nandak nandak morapmɨ aŋakwa amɨn buŋon yolgwit uŋun da but pasol awit. Yaŋ aŋakwa Yesu da paŋdetni 12 kabɨ aeni tɨmɨk paŋmuwugek yo altaŋ ɨmni uŋun dakon but pɨso yoyɨŋek
Yɨgakwa Yesu da tɨlak gen morapmɨ yoyɨŋek kɨnda yaŋ yagɨt,
Notgo do galagɨ niaŋ nandɨsal uŋun si yapmaŋek Piŋkop do galagɨ madepsi nandaŋ ɨmni. Bɨsapmɨ bɨsapmɨ uŋun do nandaŋek ae oman aŋ ɨmɨŋek egɨpni. Yaŋ aŋek gaga do but dasi niaŋ galak tosol, uŋudeŋ gɨn amɨn do but dasi galak taŋ yobi. Uŋun gen bamot da mukwa sogok mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ yapmaŋ mudomal.”
Gen uŋun yaŋba nandaŋek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nido ‘ninon bret mɨni’ yaŋ yoŋ? Gen dayɨsat uŋun dɨma nandaba pɨsosok, ma? Nandak nandak kositji sopgwit?
Yaŋ aban amɨn dɨwarɨ da kaŋek burɨ yokwi taŋba notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Nidosi pakbi kɨbaŋɨ toŋ tagɨsi uŋun yumsi tagaldak?
Muwugakwa Yesu da amɨn morapmɨsi sot mibɨlɨ mibɨlɨ awit uŋun paŋmɨlɨp agɨt. Aŋek koŋni toŋ amɨn morapmɨ koŋni yol yomgut. Aŋek koŋ uŋun nandaŋ ɨmgwit, do yaŋsop aŋyomgut.
Yaŋ yaŋek Yesu da mɨŋat monjɨyo tɨmɨgek kɨsirɨ kwenikon wɨtjɨŋek gɨsam yomgut.
Yaŋban Yesu da uŋun do bupmɨ nandaŋek kɨsitni amɨn uŋun da kwenon wɨtjɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Kɨlek toki do nandɨsat, do pasɨl gamni!”
Yesu da sot wudani toŋ morapmɨ paŋmɨlɨp agɨt, uŋun do aŋek sot wudani toŋ amɨn Yesu ɨgayɨk do aŋek ukwayɨt ukwayɨt aŋek Yesu da buron kɨwit.
Yoyɨŋakwan Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ da abɨŋ Yesu gen yokwi kɨnda yaŋban kaŋek gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋ nandaŋek yaŋ iyɨwit, “Gen tebanin da amɨn kɨnda mɨŋatni tagɨ kwɨnɨtjak do yosok bo dɨma?”
Uŋun mastat yet yombem. Mastat dakon yerɨ uŋun jap yet kɨsi morap dakon pɨŋbi, monɨŋɨsisok.
Yaŋban Yesu da gen kobogɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Gen teban mibɨltok asak uŋun yaŋ: ‘Israel amɨn kabɨ, gen uŋun nandani. Amɨn Tagɨ kaloŋ gɨn uŋun Piŋkopnin.
“Ji yo dɨwarɨ dɨ dɨma paŋek kɨni, wɨn kɨrɨŋ baŋgɨn pabɨdaŋek kɨni. Jap bo yɨk bo moneŋyo dɨma paŋek kɨni.
Bɨsit aŋek abɨŋ pɨndakban paŋdetni dɨpmɨn do yokwisi aŋek aeni dɨpmɨn sigɨn pakgwit. Paŋyolban pɨdaŋ ni gen naŋ iyɨneŋ yaŋ do ɨŋtaŋek ɨsal yɨkgwit.
Yaŋ yaŋba mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn kɨsi yaŋ gɨn notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek aŋsolat aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Amɨn dɨwarɨ paŋpulugagɨt da nido iyɨ dakon gɨptɨm aŋpulugok do aŋtɨdok asak?
Mani Yesu uŋun amɨn ɨgayɨŋ ɨmgut uŋun kok do sigɨn wɨsɨgɨt.
paŋdetni gat boron wɨgek mɨktɨm Dalmanuta tetgɨn do kɨwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda da amɨn monɨŋ kɨnda nak nandaŋ gadaŋ namɨŋakwan yokwi asak do yabekban yokwi asak kaŋ, yabet asak amɨn wit mɨsɨŋɨt tɨp madep kɨnda tegɨkon amɨn da wamaŋ maba tap ɨlarɨsigwan pɨgek tagɨ kɨmotjak.
Yaŋ yaŋek boron wɨgakwan mɨrɨm yawokgɨt. Yawogakwan paŋdetni da tamtamsi yawit.
Kɨŋ altaŋek wain gat pakbi ɨsipmɨ kɨnda mani mea gat ɨktagɨlek ɨmɨŋba nok do kurak tagɨt.
Yesu da nandak nandakni da arɨpmon Piŋkop dakon gen yoyɨŋek tɨlak gen uŋuden morapmɨ yoyɨgɨt.
Uŋun amɨn sakwabat paŋkewalek yutni tɨmɨkgaŋ. Ae amɨn da pɨndatni yaŋ do bɨsit dubagɨsi aŋ. Uŋuden amɨn gen kokwin bɨsap madepmon kobogɨ do yo jɨgɨsi pakdaŋ.”
Yaŋ iyɨŋba Yesu da pɨdaŋ agek mɨrɨm gat ae pakbi gat tebai yoyɨŋek yagɨt, “Yawokgɨl!” Yaŋban mɨrɨm yawogakwan pakbi wayɨŋ dɨmasi agɨt.
Yaŋ aŋakwa Yesu da paŋdetni tɨmɨkban pakbi ɨdapmon kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Galili amɨn morapmɨsi da yolgwit. Ae uŋun gɨn dɨma, Judia mɨktɨmon da,
Yaŋ yaŋek yagɨt, “Ji gen uŋun nandaŋ uŋun pakyaŋsi nandani. Ji Piŋkop dakon gen nandaŋek guramɨtni kaŋ, Piŋkop da saŋbeŋek damdɨsak. Mani geni dɨma nandani kaŋ, saŋbeŋek dɨma damdɨsak.
Aba uŋun akgwit kabɨkon da kɨnda da emat agak sɨbani ɨlɨkgɨt. Ɨlɨgek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon oman monjɨ mɨragɨ mandaŋ dagagɨt.
Aeni don paŋdetni 11 kabɨ muwuk yɨgek jap naŋakwa altaŋ yomgut. Altaŋ yomɨŋek gen tebaisi yaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji amɨn da ‘pɨdak da egɨsak’ yaŋ dayɨŋba nido nandaba bamɨ dɨma ak? Nandaŋ gadatji mɨni?”
Wɨkwan amɨn Yesu gat yɨkgwit uŋun da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Meŋgo padɨk padɨkgo yomakon da gak do yoŋ.”
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat mɨktɨm uŋun yɨpmaŋek Galili mɨktɨm da binapgwan kɨwit. Kɨŋakwa Yesu paŋdetni yoyɨŋdet ak do nandagɨt, do gen bini amɨn da dɨma nandani do si pasɨlek kɨwit. Aŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn Dakon Monji don amɨn da kɨsiron yɨpba aŋakba kɨmotdɨsak. Kɨmak gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Amɨn jap nawit uŋun 5 tausen yaŋ da nawit.
Yaŋ yoyɨŋek boron wɨgek pakbi ɨdap terɨ kɨnda kɨwit.
Yesu da ɨleŋ bamoron kabo noknok bamorɨ kɨsi dapgwit. Dapba Piŋkop da papiakon gen tosok uŋun bamɨ noman tagɨt. Gen uŋun yaŋ: “Yokwi pakpak amɨn uŋun kabɨkon aŋakbi.”
Ae amɨn kɨnda da wain kalugɨ tɨbɨrɨ meme gɨp baŋ wasaŋbi tɨbɨrɨ kalɨpmɨkon kolesak kaŋ uŋun tagɨ dɨma. Yaŋ asak kaŋ, wain da pukwa paptaŋ meme gɨp kɨrɨŋɨgakwa wain maŋ mudokdaŋ. Amɨn da wain kalugɨ meme gɨp kalugɨkon koleŋba wain gat meme gɨp gat kɨsi tagɨ tomal.”
Mani Yesu da mibɨlni dɨma yaŋ teŋteŋoni do yaŋsop tebaisi aŋyomgut.
Gɨldat pɨgakwan pɨlɨndo sot amɨn gat koŋni toŋ amɨn gat kɨsisi Yesukon paŋpaŋ apgwit.
Uŋudon Parisi amɨn dɨwarɨ yɨkgwit uŋun gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn. Uŋun da Yesu moneŋ tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn gat ae yokwi pakpak amɨn gat kɨsi yɨgek jap naŋba kaŋek paŋdetni yaŋ yoyɨwit, “Ma, uŋun nido takis tɨmɨt tɨmɨt amɨn gat ae yokwi pakpak amɨn gat kɨsi yɨgek jap noŋ? Uŋun tagɨ dɨma.”
Amɨn kɨnda yut kwenon egɨpjak kaŋ, yo kabɨni tɨmɨt do yutgwan dɨma pɨgɨsak.
Aŋakwan Bret Yisni Mɨni Dakon Jap Noknok Bɨsap Madep altagɨt. Uŋun bɨsapmon Israel amɨn da Yapyap Bɨlak do nandaŋek sipsip monɨŋ dapmaŋ soŋ noŋ. Uŋun bɨsapmon paŋdetni da Yesu yaŋ iyɨwit, “Nin kɨŋ dukwan Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap paŋkosit aneŋ do nandɨsal?”
“Bo namɨn dasi amɨn tebai kɨnda yɨgakwan yutnikon wɨgɨ yo kabɨni gwayeŋ tɨmɨtjak? Uŋun arɨpmɨ dɨma. Mibɨltok tebai kendagek kɨsit kandapmɨyo wamaŋek yo kabɨni tagɨ gwayeni.
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda da ɨleŋ kɨnda yaŋ iyɨsak, ‘Gak pɨdaŋ tap kaga pɨgɨ’ yaŋ iyɨŋek but bamot dɨma asak kaŋ, uŋun iyɨsak uŋudeŋ gɨn altokdɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da gen morapmɨ yaŋ ɨmgwit.
ae Jerusalem kokup papmon da, ae Idumea mɨktɨmon da, ae Jodan Pakbi usugap tet amɨn, ae Tair ae Saidon kokup tetgɨn do amɨn morapmɨ da Yesu dakon wasok agakni dakon gen bin nandaŋek apgwit.
Uŋun bɨsapmon Yesu Nasaret kokup Galili Provins yɨpmaŋek apgut. Apban Jon da Jodan Pakbikon telagɨ pakbi soŋ ɨmgut.
Uŋun Abiata da mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn egɨpgut bɨsapmon yaŋ awit. Piŋkop da yutnon wɨgek bret Piŋkop do parekbi uŋun tɨmɨk naŋek amɨn kabɨni kɨsi do yoban nawit. Bret uŋun amɨn ɨsalɨ da dɨma nok nogɨ, mukwa sogok amɨn dagɨn tagɨ nawit.”
Mani Yesu gen kagani sopmaŋek gen kobogɨ kɨnda dɨma iyɨgɨt. Yaŋ aban mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn da aeni iyɨgɨt, “Gak Kristo? Gak Piŋkop gawak ɨmamaŋ uŋun dakon Monji bo dɨma?”
Yaŋ yaŋek bɨsit tebai saŋbek saŋbek iyɨwit, “Nin nolbɨ on mɨktɨm tɨm dɨma yɨpmaŋ detneŋ.”
Ae jap yet dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm nelagɨ toŋ uŋudon maŋ kwawit. Dɨwarɨ bamɨ 100, ae dɨwarɨ bamɨ 60, ae dɨwarɨ bamɨ 30 tawit.”
Iyɨ do ‘nak Piŋkop dakon Monji’ yaŋ yosok, do ji da niaŋ aŋ ɨmneŋ do nandaŋ?” Yaŋban kɨsi morap da yawit, “Gulusuŋ asak, do si kɨmotjak.”
Betsaida kokupmon kɨŋ altaŋba amɨn dɨ da amɨn dabɨlɨ mɨni kɨnda aŋaŋ opgwit. Aŋobɨŋek Yesu da kɨsitni da wɨtjɨsak do bɨsit tebai iyɨwit.
Gɨldat binap 12 kilok aŋakwan mɨktɨm kɨsi pɨlɨn tuk aŋakwan kɨŋ pɨlɨndo 3 kilok agɨt.
Aŋakwa sakwabat yoni mɨni kɨnda da abɨŋ moneŋ gɨmani tabɨlɨ bamorɨ monɨŋɨsisok paret yopyop tamokon yopgut.
Iyɨŋ mudaŋba amɨn morapmɨsi kɨŋ abɨŋ abɨŋ aŋakwa Yesu gat yabekbi kabɨni gat jap noknok dakon bɨkbɨk dɨma pɨsaŋ yomgut. Aban Yesu da yabekbi kabɨni yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Opba mɨktɨm amɨn dɨma ekwaŋ tɨmon kɨno. Uŋudon egek tapmɨm pani.”
Wɨsa dagokdo 9 kilok aŋakwan aŋakgwit.
Uŋudeŋ gɨn yo morap dayɨt uŋun da altaŋakwa mɨktɨm da mudosak bɨsap madep kɨlɨ uŋunjok kwaŋ tosok yaŋ nandani.
Jap yet tɨŋtɨŋaŋakwan dɨwarɨ da kosiron maŋba mɨnam da abɨŋ nawit.
Amɨn morap uŋun moneŋni morapmɨ taŋ yomaŋakwa dɨwarɨ gɨn paret ɨdapmon yopmaŋ. Mani on mɨŋat wadak wadaksi aŋek moneŋni kɨsi yopmaŋdak. Kɨlɨ jap yumaŋ nosak moneŋni dɨ dɨma taŋ ɨmaŋ.”
Yesu uŋun kokup yɨpmaŋek Judia mɨktɨmon ae Jodan Pakbi terɨ kɨnda uŋudon kɨgɨt. Uŋudon egakwan mɨŋat amɨn madepsi apgwit. Apba Yesu iyɨ aŋ aŋ agɨt uŋudeŋ ae Piŋkop gen yoyɨgɨt.
Yaŋban Yesu da yaŋ yagɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda da nak do ae Gen Bin Tagɨsi do nandaŋek yutni, peni padɨk padɨkyo, sami, meŋi, datni, mɨŋat monjɨyoni, ae mɨktɨmni yopmaŋ detjak kaŋ,
Bɨsap kɨndakon peni padɨge 7 kabɨ egɨpgwit. Mibɨltok nani uŋun mɨŋat paŋek monji mɨni egek kɨmakgɨt.
Aŋakwa Pita uŋun yut da nagalgwan egakwan mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn dakon oman mɨŋatjok kɨnda da opgut.
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni burɨ yokwi taŋba kaloŋ kaloŋ yaŋ yawit, “Nak dɨma, ma?”
Amɨn uŋun sɨŋtaŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Nak amɨn pɨndakdat. Mani pɨndakgo kɨndap yombem da obɨgɨ abɨgɨyo yaŋ aŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek kɨndap kɨrɨŋ naŋ busuŋɨkon aŋagek ɨlɨp sul ɨmgwit. Yaŋ aŋek gawak ɨmɨŋek toptopmon da man madep ɨmgwit.
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak asisi dayɨsat, on akgaŋ kabɨkon dɨ dɨma kɨmagek Piŋkop dakon Amɨn Kɨla Agakni tapmɨmɨ toŋsi apban kokdaŋ.”
Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn aŋgwasɨŋek yɨkgwit kabɨkon dabɨl sɨŋtaŋek yagɨt, “Nak dakon meŋno ae padɨk padɨkno oni.
Ji da Piŋkop bɨsit iyɨŋba nandaŋakwan yo uŋun ais bɨsapmon dɨma altoni.
“Aba, Dat, gak da yo morap tagɨ aki. Do nak da kwenon jɨgɨ apdɨsak uŋun kukwoki do nandɨsat. Mani nak dakon galaktok dɨma yolgi, gaga dakon galaktok uŋun gɨn yolgi.”
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni amɨn kabɨ madep yopmaŋ degek boron wɨkwa paŋdetni gat kɨsi kɨwit. Ae bot dɨwarɨ gat kɨsi kɨwit.
Yesu abɨdawit amɨn uŋun da Yesu abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ da yutnon wɨgɨwit. Uŋun yutnon mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn ae gen teban yoyɨŋdet ae kɨla amɨn kɨsi muwuk egɨpgwit.
Dɨwarɨ da kokup dubagɨkon da apgwit, do yabekgo kɨni kaŋ, kosiron jap do aŋek dabɨlɨ upbal taŋba maŋ potdaŋ.”
Yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “Amɨn da gadat gadat tebaisi aŋakwa namɨn da ɨgayɨŋ namɨsak yaŋ nido yosol?”
Nak asisi dayɨsat, amɨn kɨnda da mɨŋat monjɨyo da Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak abɨdoŋ uŋun da tɨlak dɨma abɨdoni kaŋ, uŋungwan arɨpmɨ dɨma pɨgɨkdaŋ.”
Yesu da kɨndap uŋun yaŋ kaŋek yagɨt, “Buŋon bamɨ dɨmasi toki, aŋaki amɨn da dɨmasi paŋ noni dosi nandɨsat.” Gen yagɨt uŋun paŋdetni da nandawit.
Kɨlek taŋban uŋudon gɨn Yesu da amɨn uŋun yabegek gen tebai yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Aŋek Yesu yutnon wɨgakwan amɨn kabɨ madepsi aeni uŋudon muwukgwit. Muwugakwa Yesu gat paŋdetni gat jap noni dakon bɨkbɨk dɨma pɨsaŋ yomgut.
Yaŋ yaŋban gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋudon yɨkgwit uŋun da burɨ da yaŋ nandawit,
Wɨsa dagaŋakwan Betani kokup yɨpmaŋ dek obɨŋ kosiron Yesu jap do agɨt.
Yaŋban notni yoyɨŋ yoyɨŋ aŋek yaŋ yawit, “Ninon bret mɨni uŋun do bo yosok?”
Aŋakwa Yesu da amɨn kɨsirɨ gɨreŋɨkbi yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Amɨn da ɨŋamon pɨdaŋ at.”
Jon dakon paŋdetni gat ae Parisi amɨn gat uŋun bɨsapmon Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egɨpgwit. Aŋakwa amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋun Yesukon kɨŋek yaŋ iyɨwit: “Jon dakon paŋdetni gat ae Parisi amɨn dakon paŋdetni gat uŋun Piŋkop do nandaŋek jap kelek egakwa gak dakon paŋdetgoni nido jap naŋek ekwaŋ?”
“Ji niaŋ nandaŋ? Don pi ami da abɨŋ pi kɨla amɨn niaŋ aŋyomjak? Pi ami da abɨŋ uŋun kɨla amɨn dapban kɨmotdaŋ. Dapban kɨmagakwa wain pi uŋun amɨn ŋwakŋwarɨ da kɨsiron yɨpdɨsak.
Yaŋ yaŋban nandaŋek mukwa sogok amɨn dakon mibɨltok amɨn iyɨ dakon paba pɨgɨkni pudagɨt. Yaŋ aŋek yagɨt, “Mibɨlni nandak do amɨn nido saŋbeŋek yoyɨno apni?
Amɨn Dakon Monji uŋun mɨktɨmon dɨwarɨ wɨrɨrɨt dakon pi asak do yaŋ mudaŋ ɨbi yaŋ nandaba pɨsosak do on amɨn aŋmɨlɨp abeŋ.” Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn kɨsirɨ kandapmɨyo kɨmakbi yaŋ iyɨgɨt,
Yesu da saŋbeŋek yaŋ yagɨt, “Piŋkop da Amɨn Kɨla Asak uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ yo nikon tɨlak ako nandani?
Kɨmagakwa bɨt dakon kɨla amɨn da kokup kapmat tagɨt ae mɨktɨm dɨwarɨkon kɨŋ yo uŋun noman tawit dakon gen bin yoyɨwit. Yoyɨŋba amɨn da yo noman tagɨt uŋun kok do aŋek abɨŋ mudawit.
Egakwan mɨrɨm madep aŋakwan paŋdetni pakbi wayɨt do aŋtɨdok aŋakwa pɨndakgɨt. Yaŋ pɨndagek wɨsa wɨsa do pakbi ɨdapmon bamaŋ bamaŋ kɨŋek kɨŋ paŋdetni yap do agɨt.
(Amɨn jap nawit uŋun 4 tausen yaŋ da nawit.) Yaŋ aŋek Yesu da mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep yabekban kɨŋakwa,
Yaŋba Yesu da yoyɨgɨt, “Dewit ae amɨn kabɨni jap do aŋek yo awit uŋun ji manjɨŋ nandaŋyo awit bo dɨma?
Aban mɨŋat uŋun da Yesu dakon bin nandaŋek, mɨŋat amɨn dɨwarɨ uŋun da bɨkbɨgon egek manjikon kɨŋek ɨlɨkba pɨgɨknikon ɨgayɨgɨt.
Uŋun amɨn kabɨ da aŋsolat aŋek, ɨlɨp sul ɨmɨŋek, baljaŋek aŋakba kɨmotjak. Gɨldat kapbɨ aŋakwan kɨmoron da pɨdokdɨsak.”
Mani mɨktɨmon kwaotno madepsi kwosok. Jap dɨwarɨ dakon tagok tagokni uŋun yapmaŋ mudosok. Kɨlɨŋɨ madep yopban kɨŋakwa mɨnam morapmɨ da paŋabɨŋ uŋun da yoŋgamgwan yɨkgaŋ.”
Yo jɨgɨsi morap uŋun dɨma altaŋakwa wagɨl dayɨsat, do dɨsi kaŋ kɨmotni.”
Mani don monjɨ uŋun abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ kɨŋakwa notni uŋun bɨsapmon jap kelek ekwaŋ.
Kokup kɨndakon kɨŋ altaŋba not dɨma aŋdamɨŋek genji dɨma nandaŋek manji damni kaŋ, kandapjikon kɨmbabaŋ toŋ uŋun kokup yɨp do aŋek tɨdaŋba kɨni. Yaŋ aŋakwa uŋun kokup amɨn da ‘Geni dɨma nandamaŋ, uŋun do aŋ’ yaŋ nandani.”
“Uŋun bɨsapmon amɨn kɨnda da ‘Kristo oni!’ bo ‘Asoni!’ yaŋ yaŋban kaŋ, geni dɨma nandaŋ gadani.
Ae uŋun da buŋon yaŋ tosok: ‘Gaga do but dasi niaŋ galak tosol, uŋudeŋ gɨn amɨn do but dasi galak taŋ yobi.’ Uŋun gen teban bamot da gen teban morap yapmaŋ mudomal.”
Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn monɨŋ kɨnda abɨdaŋ aŋobɨŋ bɨkbɨknikon yɨpban agakwan kɨsirɨ da abɨdaŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt,
Wɨgɨ mɨŋatjok kɨsirɨkon abɨdaŋek iyɨgɨt, “Talita kum!” (Uŋun dakon mibɨlɨ, “Mɨŋatjok pɨdoki do gayɨsat!”)
Yesu gat paŋdetni gat Jerusalem kɨŋ altawit. Kɨŋ altaŋek Yesu Telagɨ Yut Madep da nagalgwan pɨgɨ pɨndakban amɨn moneŋ ɨlɨt pi awit. Uŋun wasaŋek amɨn yolban waŋga abɨgɨwit. Yaŋ aŋek moneŋ kulabɨk awit amɨn dakon tamo, ae mɨnam baŋ moneŋ ɨlɨt awit amɨn dakon tamo uŋun kɨsi paŋtobɨlban tagal kɨwit.
Kɨŋ altaŋakwa Yesu boron da ɨleŋɨkon obɨŋek amɨn morapmɨsi pɨndagek sipsip kɨla amɨni mɨni yombem da egɨpgwit, do bupmɨsi nandaŋ yomgut. Yaŋ nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn wasaŋek Piŋkop gen morapmɨ yoyɨgɨt.
Naŋba arɨpmɨ aŋakwan bret dɨwat ae tap kɨlap dɨwat tawit uŋun paŋdetni da yɨk madepsi 12 kabɨ sɨmɨlba tugawit.
Ae amɨn dɨwarɨ mɨktɨm nap kelɨ toŋ tɨm yombem. Uŋun Piŋkop gen nandaŋ,
Yesu pɨdaŋ kɨk do aŋakwan amɨn kɨnda tɨmtɨm yaŋek abɨŋ gawak ɨmɨŋek yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Yoyɨŋdet gɨman, niaŋsi aŋek egɨp egɨp dagok dagogɨ mɨni abɨdokeŋ?”
Emat amɨn da Yesu abɨdaŋ aŋaŋ gapman yut madep da nagalgwan pɨgɨwit. Pɨgek emat amɨn notni dɨwarɨ kɨsisi yaŋ yoba abɨŋ mudawit.
Amɨn madep kabɨkon Piŋkop gen tɨlak genon dagɨn yoyɨgɨt. Mani paŋdetni gat egek tɨlak gen dakon mibɨlɨ yoyɨŋ teŋteŋagɨt.
Uŋun da Sabat bɨsapmon amɨn paŋmɨlɨp aban kaŋek gen pikon yɨpneŋ yaŋon da amɨn dɨwarɨ Yesu tebai kaŋek yɨkgwit.
Yaŋ iyɨŋban mɨŋat uŋun yutnikon kɨŋ kaŋban gwi koŋni mɨni da tamokon pakban kagɨt.
Yaŋ yaŋek amɨn kabɨ madep yopmaŋek yutnon wɨgakwan paŋdetni da tɨlak gen dakon mibɨlɨ nandak do iyɨwit.
Muwut muwut yutnikon ae jap noknok bɨsap madepmon amɨn mani toŋ da yɨyɨt tamokon yɨt do galak toŋ.
Uwal da kɨsiron yɨpyɨp amɨn da gen kɨnda kɨlɨ yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Amɨn kɨnda nak da mandaŋ noko kaŋ, uŋun amɨn naŋ abɨdoni. Abɨdaŋek kɨlani tebai aŋek aŋaŋ kɨni.”
Pailat yaŋ yagɨt nido iyɨ nandagɨt: mukwa sogok amɨn dakon amɨn madep kabɨ Yesu do nandaba yokwi taŋban top yaŋek gen pikon yɨpgwit.
Iyɨŋban nandaŋek Yesu gat kɨgɨmal. Kɨŋakwal amɨn morapmɨ da yolek gadat gadat tebaisi awit.
Dewit da uŋun amɨn do Amɨn Tagɨ yaŋ iyɨgɨt, do Kristo uŋun Dewit dakon yawi dɨwatni dɨma, uŋun Amɨn Tagɨni.” Yesu da gen uŋun yaŋakwan mɨŋat amɨn kabɨ madep da nandaŋ galak tawit.
Gen uŋun nandaŋek uŋudon gɨn terɨ terɨ sɨŋtaŋek amɨn bamot ae dɨma pɨndakgwit. Yesu iyɨ gɨn kawit.
Yaŋba Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji Piŋkop da papiakon gen tosok uŋun dɨma kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋ. Ae Piŋkop dakon teban tok tosok uŋun kɨsi dɨma kaŋ nandaŋyo aŋ. Uŋun do aŋek ji gen gulusuŋ yoŋ.
Yaŋ yaŋek aŋgwikon kɨŋ mɨktɨmon maŋ pagek bɨsit agɨt. Kosit kɨnda tosagon uŋun bɨsap yokwi yapjak yaŋ nandaŋek bɨsit yaŋ yagɨt,
“Uŋun do aŋek ji kaŋ kɨmotni. Ji yut dakon ami ni bɨsapmon apjak uŋun dɨma nandaŋ. Apjak bɨsap uŋun pɨlɨndo bo kalbi binap bo pup da gen yosok bɨsapmon bo wɨsa dagokdo uŋun ji dɨma nandaŋ.
Yaŋba yoyɨgɨt, “Koŋ uŋuden uŋun yum yolyolɨ dɨma. Bɨsiron da tagɨ yolyolɨ.”
Yoyɨŋban kokupmon kɨŋ Yesu da yo morap do yoyɨgɨt uŋudeŋsi pɨndakgɨmal. Yaŋ pɨndagek Yapyap Bɨlak dakon jap paŋkosit agɨmal.
Gen uŋun nandaŋek Yesu da yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji nandaŋ gadatji mɨni amɨn nak bɨsap niaŋ da ji gat egɨpbeŋ? Ae bɨsap niaŋ da ji dakon jɨgɨ guramɨkgeŋ? Monjɨ uŋun nagon aŋopgut.”
Aeni saŋbeŋek yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Ji mɨktɨmɨ mɨktɨmɨ kɨŋ Gen Bin Tagɨsi amɨn kɨsisi yoyɨŋ mudoni.
Yaŋba yaŋ yoyɨgɨt, “Nak uŋun amɨn kabɨ dogɨn dɨma pɨgɨm. Do nin kokup taŋ aŋaŋ kwaŋ uŋudon kɨŋek Piŋkop gen yoyɨkeŋ. Nak pi uŋun ak do pɨgɨm.”
Yaŋ yaŋek aeni tobɨlek kɨŋ bɨsit mibɨltok agɨt uŋudeŋ gɨn agɨt.
Gen teban yoyɨŋdet amɨn da tɨlagon dɨma yagɨt, amɨn mani toŋ da tɨlagon yagɨt, do amɨn da Piŋkop gen yogokni do nandaba ŋwakŋwarɨsi agɨt.
Uŋun amɨn bamot kɨŋ donki bɨlagɨ uŋun kosiron kagɨmal. Uŋun amɨn kɨnda da yoma kagakon gwɨlɨkba akgɨt. Napmɨ wɨtdalbal,
Iyɨŋban Yesu da yaŋ iyɨgɨt, “Mibɨltok Juda amɨn paŋpulugaŋek ae don mɨktɨm dɨwarɨkon amɨn paŋpulugokeŋ. Yosol uŋudeŋ abeŋ kaŋ, mɨŋat monjɨyo dakon jap pɨŋan do yomdɨsat. Uŋun tagɨ dɨma.”
Yaŋ yaŋban paŋdetni da yaŋ iyɨwit, “On ekwamaŋon amɨn dɨma ekwaŋ, do jap dukon baŋ paŋabɨŋ on mɨŋat amɨn madep yomneŋ?”
Kɨŋ altaŋban wain pi dakon kɨla amɨn da uŋun pi monjɨ abɨdaŋ aŋagek bamɨ kɨnda dɨma ɨmɨŋek yɨpba kɨgɨt.
Uŋun yokwi morap amɨn buron da wɨŋ waŋga kwaŋ uŋun da amɨn paŋupbal aŋ.”
Uŋun bɨsapmon mɨŋat kɨnda gwi koŋni toŋ uŋun da Yesu dakon gen bini nandaŋek abɨŋ Yesu da kandap mibɨlon gawak ɨmgut.
Nak pakbisi baŋ telagɨ pakbi soŋ damɨsat, mani uŋun da Telagɨ Wup soŋ damdɨsak.”
Yaŋ yaŋek yagɨt, “Tɨlak gen yat dakon mibɨlɨ dɨma nandaŋ kaŋ, tɨlak gen dɨwarɨ yoko niaŋ aŋek nandaŋ pɨsoni?
